<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_10190995-1656-4bd8-8076-8b100aff1f6b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer16523077782376425113"><i>From <b>New York Times</b> and <b>USA Today</b> bestselling author <b>Aleatha Romig</b> comes the thrilling sequel in the <b>Consequences</b> series: <b>Truth</b>, a game of deception, intrigue, and conspiracy where losing can be deadly.</i><br/><br/><b>Claire survived the consequences. </b><br/><br/>Through strength and compartmentalization, Claire Nichols captivated her captor.   <span id="freeText16523077782376425113" style="display:none"><i>From <b>New York Times</b> and <b>USA Today</b> bestselling author <b>Aleatha Romig</b> comes the thrilling sequel in the <b>Consequences</b> series: <b>Truth</b>, a game of deception, intrigue, and conspiracy where losing can be deadly.</i><br /><br /><b>Claire survived the consequences. </b><br /><br />Through strength and compartmentalization, Claire Nichols captivated her captor. Though Anthony Rawlings thought he taught Claire to behave, his domination became desire, and his obsession morphed into love. Or was it? When her choices pushed Anthony's relentless vendetta too far, Claire barely survived the consequences. <br /><br /><b>Discover the truth.</b><br /><br />Now, armed with new information and more questions than answers, Claire works to uncover the truth behind the dangerous game at play. As she begins anew, she must decide whom she can truly trust, especially with a new set of players on the move.<br /><br /><b>New set of rules.</b><br /><br />With everything to lose and a manipulative game master controlling the board, Claire and Tony duel by a new set of rules. When thrust together once again, can they learn to trust each other to overcome new dangers? Or will this be Tony's second attempt at domination? Can Claire resist the man she'd never before been able to resist? Hatred and love. Deception and truth. Old habits and new beginnings. As this real-life game of chess plays out, past sins will come to light and new secrets will be revealed. With so much riding on each move, the stakes have never been higher.<br /><br /><i>All truths are easy to understand once they are discovered. The trick is to discover them. <b>- Galileo</b></i></span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I think we can all *try*, and, as social animals, we want to fit in, but anyone with any awareness of neuroscience and psychology knows that there are<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I think we can all *try*, and, as social animals, we want to fit in, but anyone with any awareness of neuroscience and psychology knows that there are very REAL limits to what people can be trained to do. What if Claire had depression? Bipolar disorder? Autism spectrum? Fragile bones? Hemophilia? Progressive MS? Lupus? What if she was already *broken* before Tony got to her? What would he have done then? <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer520910144" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3269475063379147851"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407327i/795501._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b> I swear to God, this book should come with a care package – tequila, Valium, a stress ball and a punching bag. Just sayin’ !! </b><br/><br/>This review has no plot-related spoilers in it. Rating: 4.5 stars.<br/><br/><b> Honestly, </b> when I was about to start reading this, I was just wondering where on EARTH could the story go from that point?? How could the mindfuck POSSIBLY get any deeper?<br/><br/>The facts were there. Actions had been taken. And I was absolutely positive that I hated Tony Rawlings. Like really, really hated!! I w</span>
  <span id="freeText3269475063379147851" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407327i/795501._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b> I swear to God, this book should come with a care package – tequila, Valium, a stress ball and a punching bag. Just sayin’ !! </b><br><br>This review has no plot-related spoilers in it. Rating: 4.5 stars.<br><br><b> Honestly, </b> when I was about to start reading this, I was just wondering where on EARTH could the story go from that point?? How could the mindfuck POSSIBLY get any deeper?<br><br>The facts were there. Actions had been taken. And I was absolutely positive that I hated Tony Rawlings. Like really, really hated!! I was sure he belonged in a jail cell and no where else. I mean… looooook what he did! Right? Riiiight?? …<br><br>WRONG.<br><br>Le sigh *deep breath*<br><br><b> Over the course of this book, my emotions were toyed with, and my heart was lead down a path I would have SWORN it would never go down. </b> <br><br>I have to say that, having finished the book, I am officially on Team Tony ((I think)).<br><br>Whaaaat?? O_O<br><br>I’m sure any of you who have only read book #1 think I’m utterly insane now. I’m not. I swear. Just… stuff happened. Big stuff. Changes. Growth. An understanding. And in the end, I have to say that, honestly, I’m not 100% sold on the Team Tony thing, but… I’m about 95% there. Honestly, I don’t think there is ANYTHING in the entire world that will EVER make me able to be 100% in love with him. Why? Because of what he did in Consequences.<br><br>Having read Truth, I feel like I’ve come to have a deeper understanding for him. And a respect for the changes he made. BUT. Nothing can ever erase the past. The future can still be determined, but the past is fixed. And because of that, no matter WHAT he does, there will always be a small 5% of me on guard because I *know* that somewhere in that man lies (or, lay) the potential to make the events of Consequences happen. But… so long as those old actions never resurface, I am willing to be open-minded and accept the new Tony for who he is.<br><br>So, I’ll revise my statement…. <b> I am officially <u> Team (new) Tony </u>. That is my team. </b> #teamNEWtony<br><br><br><br><br><i> <b> “Love and hate are very close emotions. Both intense and consuming”<br><br>“Could it be possible to hate and love someone too?“ </b></i>  <br><br>I have to say that Ms Romig is an very talented author not only because the story is good, but in large part its because of the actual writing style – its an extremely well written book.<br><br>Did I dread going into this book? Yeah. A little. I wasn’t sure how far the mind fuck would go. Or if I was ready to handle it. But I bravely put my big girl panties on and dove in and seriously, woah!<br><br>There’s no ‘easing’ into this book. Nope! The prologue pretty much just slams you into the story and away you go – its a <b> roller coaster </b> ride of questions, more questions, the occasional answer, which in turn leads to more questions… I will say though, that we did make some big ‘discoveries’ in this book. It kept me guessing but I was pleased to see some of my theories work out too.<br><br>I was just in this constant state of… <i> Wait, could it be him who did that? But then, why would he have done the other thing?? … Hmmm *wonders* …. </i> Its this complete feeling of not knowing which way is up. Not being able to tell right from wrong.<br><br><b> Do the ends justify the means? </b> I felt myself constantly asking myself that.<br><br>After the events of the last book, I’d become jumpy and deeply <b> mistrustful </b>. <u> Of everyone. </u> Now, every single thing was squinted at suspiciously, every possible action was eyed from all angles to try and figure out if it had a double meaning or a hidden purpose.<br><br>I have to say that, as a romance reader, I am usually either bored to tears by the ‘mystery’ side of stories but that was NOT the case with this one. I was really riveted to the story. It was so multi layered and multi dimensional with so many possibilities and outcomes that I found myself just needing to know the answers.<br><br>That being said, I will say that this book “felt” <b> long </b> . Its not a bad thing, or a complaint, but I found it a longer book to get through than the first one. Kind of like with book #1, I reached a point around 60% in where I was definitely intrigued and invested in the story, but no longer had any idea where it was going. But once again, once I got to the final 20% I just couldn’t look away!!<br><br>This story had double <b> layers </b> to everything. The double layers even had layers… it was this spiral downward into more and more questions………<br><br>I don’t know how to explain how HARD the little reveals hit me. Every time we actually learned something that was a fact, a definitive piece to the puzzle, I got that same full body CHILLLLLLS feeling. It was pretty cool <br><br>I liked that we got bits and pieces from all sorts of perspectives in this book. It was still primarily Claire’s story, but there was a LOT of back story into Tony’s early years that gave us a much better understanding of him and the complexity of where the plot originated (gosh, that’s vague, lol), and there were some side characters that got their perspective told to help round out the story as well.<br><br><b> Tony’s back story </b> was one of my favorite parts because we got to see the life events that made him into the kind of person he was. I found it gave a lot of insight into his character and, although it didn’t excuse any of his actions, it DID help me understand him more.<br><br>I liked that in this book we got to see more of Claire’s strength shine though. She’d been through hell and now, despite her traumas was at a place where she was regaining a measure of control over her life. She was brave and smart about many things but there were still some moments of naivety where I wanted to shake her, moments where I couldn’t understand *why* she’d go along with something or make the decisions she made. She frustrated me in places but I got to a place where I felt I understood her a lot more.<br><br>And then there was Harry. The anti-Tony. Was I in love with him? Hmmm, a little bit. Ok, fine, a lot. And I think that if Tony hadn’t changed, I would have loved him more. But… gah, I mean, he was kind of perfect. And I totally could see myself falling for him. I was soooooooo tempted by him! So. Freaking. Tempted!! but… the sick twisted part of my mind is grumbling over the fact that he’s just not Tony so… even though, I will admit, there was a chunk of the book where I kind of was rooting for him, my heart ended up choosing Tony.<br><br>About Tony though….. *deep breath* I really felt like my emotions went though a long journey with him in this book. <b> In my heart, I wanted to ‘fix’ him. </b> Tried to justify things. But my brain thankfully kept stepping in and reminding me of everything he’d done in book #1 (and even, to an extent, book #2). I mean, where is the line drawn? The line after which the guy is just too fucked up to fix? Had he crossed it? … well, yes. But… could he still change? Well… apparently so!<br><br>He toyed with my emotions again in this book though because just when I thought he was turning over a new leaf, he’d AGAIN go overboard and leave me spluttering and wanting to throttle him.<br><br>I couldn’t tell if he was still being manipulative or if I should try and forgive him… Was he even WORTHY of forgiveness? His actions in book #1 were unforgivable in my eyes.<br><br>What if this was the story of the attempted redemption of an irredeemable man?<br><br>I wanted to love him. I loved his spark. I loved his intentions… but actions speak louder than words and a lot of his were just MESSED up. Not. Okay. There are some things you just can’t justify. But… what if its not about justification. What if it was about change? He WAS trying. That was impossible to deny. But… was the change enough?<br><br>Love should never be forced. Or bought. Or coerced… <b> but what happens when you’re faced with someone who doesn’t know HOW to love. </b> Who has never known it. Never been shown it. And never experienced it. Who had wrapped himself in a security blanket of control. Given his back story, I could see where his dominance came from – he had such a deepseeded insecurity and fear stemming form a lack of a love and a fear of the loss of the only shred of love he’s ever know that his actions were, to me, for the first time, understandable as opopsed to flat-out crazy (even though I still didn’t agree with them all).<br><br>He just didn’t know HOW to love having never really BEEN loved ever.<br><br>There was a turning point. A definitive turning point after which the change he made in himself was undeniable. He tempered himself, controlled himself and was put in many situations where he had the opportunity to go all old-Tony-psycho on us but he didn’t. To me, he was showing his self control and how strong his desire to be the kind of person Claire deserved was.<br><br>Also, the more he changed, and the more ‘sane’ his actions became, the more I beganto see the world through his eyes more. He became a lot easier to relate too and I even found myself supporting many of his decisions that I might, in the past, have frowned upon because I could ‘get’ where he was coming from.<br><br>I even got to the point where I was flat-out AWWW-ing and grinning over some of his lines and scenes with Claire. Seriously guys! I even had a heart clench moment for him!! A heart clench!!!! Never thought I’d see that day.<br><br><b> I decided that you can’t fix the past or turn back time. But you CAN decide the future. </b> <br><br>I do not take back any of my previous Tony-hating feelings from before. Those ALL remain the same. Yes, I hated him and truly believed he deserved to rot in a jail cell. But… as he changed, so did my feelings.<br><br>So yeah… given his changes and proof in certain scenarios which would have sent the old-Tony into a flying rage, but the new-Tony handled with an attitude I could understand and respect…. I have fallen for him.<br><br>I’m decidedly on <b> <u> Team (new) Tony. </u> </b> #teamNEWtony<br><br>But let me tell you…. if he puts one TOE wrong in CONVICTED…. *shakes fist* . Let’s just say that my new “team” alliance is built on faith and trust and not much else and because of his past, it would be pretty easy to have that come crumbling down so I’m just saying…<br><br>About the ending… I know some of you will be wondering if its a cliffhanger so I’ll let you know there is clearly a TON more to the story – lots of secrets still to unravel, a lot more questions to answer, and of course a “conviction” to be made, BUT.. <b> it ended at a point I could live with. </b> I’m okay to wait at this point. The characters are all at a place where, in my mind, I’m okay to leave them until the next book is out.<br><br>Speaking of the next book, <b> CONVICTED, </b> it is due out late 2013/early 2014 at this point. If that changes, I’ll keep you guys informed <br><br>Here’s a break down of some of my reactions while reading… Spoiler-free of course!<br><br><u> 27% </u> - Ohhhhh FUCK. Guess that’s a lesson never to underestimate Tony! GURK!!<br><br><u> 30% </u> - Hmm there’s that *spark* again with Tony. Dammit. WHY AM I FALLING FOR IT?????? Cuz I so am :/<br><br><u> 33% </u> - O_O<br><br><u> 39% </u> - DAMMIT!! I swore this wouldn’t happen but yes, Tony is melting my heart just a wee bit.<br><br><u> 45% </u> - Grrrrr Tony, dammit, stop making it so hard to love you!!!! *mimes throttling*<br><br><u> 58% </u> - *blink* … *blink*<br><br><u> 69% </u> - SAY WHAAAAA???? Gahhhhh!!!! Ok This brings a whole extra level of NOT OKAY to the already high levels of NOT OKAY surrounding the dream thing. Just sayin’!<br><br><u> 78% </u> - Ok. I’m officially leaning towards Team (reformed) Tony now… Tony, pleasepleaseplease don’t make me hate you again!!! *whispers* #TeamTony<br><br><u> 80% </u> - Awwwwwww!!! Seriously, I can’t believe I’m awww-ing but I totally am.<br><br><u> 84% </u> - FFUUUUCCCKKKKKKKK!!!!<br><br><u> 89% </u> - *grins* seriously, AWWWWWWW<br><br><u> 92% </u> - HOLYYY FUCKING HELL!!!! OMG! I so so SO called it!!!!<br><br><u> 97% </u> - Pleasedontbeacliffhanger pelasedontbeacliffhanger pleasedontbeacliffhanger pleasepleasepleasepleasepleeeeeease<br><br><u> 100% </u> - *deeeeep breath* okay. I’m okay with it ending there. I FREAKING WANT THE NEXT BOOK. but I’m okay to wait…. *whew*<br><br>Teehee.<br><br><b> If I had to rate it, I’d give it the same rating as book #1 –&gt; 4.5 stars. </b><br><br>Here's my casting for Tony and Claire:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791760i/554483._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394939i/760561._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539275765?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539275765" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13426408308883896962">Find This and Other Reviews At <a href='http://cravestheangst.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Craves The Angst</a>.<br/><br/><b>1 Deflated Disappointed Star!</b><br/><b>
  <i>I Must Tell The TRUTH!</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Beware of the Spoilers Below…and Warning of Long Winded Ranting!</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>The Review:</i>
</b><br/>If you read my review for this series’ first book, <i>Consequences</i>, you know that I didn’t think favorably of it. In fact, I only gave it two stars because of how much I disliked both main characters, Anthony and Claire and I wasn’t inclined to move on to book two and subject myself to another read that left me feeling </span>
  <span id="freeText13426408308883896962" style="display:none">Find This and Other Reviews At <a href="http://cravestheangst.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Craves The Angst</a>.<br /><br /><b>1 Deflated Disappointed Star!</b><br /><b>
  <i>I Must Tell The TRUTH!</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Beware of the Spoilers Below…and Warning of Long Winded Ranting!</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>The Review:</i>
</b><br />If you read my review for this series’ first book, <i>Consequences</i>, you know that I didn’t think favorably of it. In fact, I only gave it two stars because of how much I disliked both main characters, Anthony and Claire and I wasn’t inclined to move on to book two and subject myself to another read that left me feeling desolate and empty. But I was assured that I would feel completely different about <u>Truth</u> and by the end of the book I would be “Team Tony”. So against my better judgment, I moved on to book two with hope and an open mind. Partnering with my favorite gal pal, Juls, we did this as a buddy read, so we could rant or rave as we read through each chapter.<br /> <br />Well, as I sit here trying to come up with what to say in this review, the only phrase I can come up with is…<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I Call Bullshit!</i>
</b><br /><br /><u>Truth</u> had me wishing I could rewind time and get back the hours I spent trapped inside this tortuous, infuriating read!<br /><br />If it’s even possible, this book was worse than the first book, leaving me with no choice but to hide behind the masses of four and five star raters with my lonely one star rating.<br /> <br />And I have one question…<br /><br /><i>What in the hell did everyone see in this book that I didn’t?</i><br /><br />I know I’m in the minority here but if you’ll continue to read I’ll share my thoughts and why I thought it didn’t warrant praise from this reviewer. <br /><br /><i>The Story…</i><br />First let me say, the first fifty percent of the book was great! By some stroke of luck and a dying judge’s attempt at revenge, Claire is released from prison. With the help of her lawyer, a mysterious benefactor and an old friend, Claire sneaks away from Iowa where she’s spent the last three years in purgatory. She gets to the sunny shores of California where she starts a new and beautiful life filled with the love of good friends, family reconnections and even a new love interest. Things seem to be going in the right direction for Claire and with her mind set on her new life as well as utilizing her new-found detective skills, she seek out information on her ex-husband, Anthony, knowing knowledge is power. Certain its only a matter of time before Anthony finally finds her, she wants to be ready to combat whatever his next move is. She knows her life is a game of chess to the domineering and vile Anthony and with her friends and family, she gains a strength she hasn’t known in a long time. <br /><br />And then the book takes a one-eighty down the path of “I can’t believe this shit!”. In walks Anthony into Claire’s new life and everything goes <i>BOOM</i>! Instead of stealing her away in the middle of the night and trapping her in his mansion in Iowa as he did before, Anthony worms his way back into her life spouting promises of love and being a changed man. <br /><br />And Claire, instead of being revolted by her kidnapper, rapist, abuser and armed with the knowledge or at least the suspicion of his past deeds as a murderer, Claire decides this <i>poor man</i> has had such a horrific childhood by stumbling across the bodies of his murdered parents, that surely he’s scarred and in need of a big ol’ Claire hug! *sigh* Soon her resolve for vengeance for all this evil man has done to her, vanishes and in its place is sympathy, concern and the idiotic notion that he couldn’t, nor will he ever hurt her again!<br /><br />And while she’s running about defending this man who destroys lives everywhere he goes, he’s out continuing to plot his revenge on the next unsuspecting person. <br /><br /><b>THIS BOOK WAS STUPID!!!</b><br /><br /><i>Characters…</i><br />Anthony’s reasoning for wanting revenge in the name of his grandfather is way stupid! Nathaniel’s unsavory business practices start this whole mess by stealing money that wasn’t his! And when he gets caught, he rages how he’s going to seek revenge on those who turned him in but before he gets a chance to do so, he dies in prison… where he BELONGED! So Anthony and Nathaniel’s young wife take up the gauntlet to exact his revenge on his behalf. Time and money are the only things standing in their way so they wait and Anthony builds his empire. When the timing is right, they start killing off family members of the two men who turned Nathaniel in. Marie and Anthony’s vengeance was just self-indulgent and dumb.<br /> <br />Anthony isn’t a complicated character. He isn’t a beautiful soul hidden behind a rough exterior. He’s completely ruthless and insane! He’s a petty, childish man with control issues who’s pouting because someone stole his favorite toy and now he's throwing mud in everyone’s sandbox! Ugg!!! <b>I HATE HIM!!!</b> Even if his reasons weren’t completely ridiculous, his methods were irredeemable!!! I could <i>NEVER</i> find him attractive! He kidnaps Claire, he rapes her repeatedly until she submits through fear, he beats her into a two week coma where she suffers a concussion, broken ribs and broken bones and he puts such a whammy on her mind, she actually thinks she’s in love with him. He intimidates her through fear and domination. He ruined her sisters life by ensuring her brother-in-law, John, lost his prominent lawyers career and Emily lost her teaching job by having to move once John was thrown in jail for a crime he didn’t commit. One in which Anthony set him up for. Anthony is implicated in Simon’s death. Claire suspects he could have had something to do with her own parent’s death. And most importantly, Anthony sets Claire up for his attempted murder and sends her to prison!!! His crimes are countless and extend further than I can list here on this review. <br /><br />Why in the hell would Claire want him? How could she love a man who’s done all these things to HER? Is she just an idiot with no common sense or mind of her own or is she a masochist who gets off on the pain and misery? And what’s worse, throughout <u>Truth</u>, Claire gives up her new love interest Harry, a man who cherished her and was honorable. She actually gets upset with her sister and her brother-in-law for trying to talk her out of going back to Anthony. There were several times she puts off talking to Emily and flat out refusing to tell her sister the truth. Emily, who was there for her through everything, who suffered as much as Claire, even if not physically, is now a nuisance to Claire because she wants <b>good</b> things for Claire instead a life of <b>fear and degradation</b>. <br /><br />Claire is a selfish bitch! This chick, by not telling the truth and not trying to change her circumstances in <i>Consequences</i> and by going back to Anthony after everything he’s done to her and her entire family, has once again pushed the unconditional love and support away to be with a man who was the reason for all the bad and horrific things in her life. <br /><br />And then if all that wasn’t bad enough, the mystery surrounding the revenge in this book fell flat and was entirely too predictable. Another thing that irritated me was Claire seemed to be the pied piper of men. Whoever came into contact with her, wanted her. She must have had beer flavored nipple or something because Anthony wanted her to the point of insanity, Harry wanted to be with her and then the PI who Anthony hired fell in love with her. I’m sorry, but there was NOTHING special about Claire let alone enough to warrant man after man falling at her feet in worship. <br /><br />Also, the ending of this book sucked and the fact Claire leaves town letting her sister think she’s been kidnapped again or is dead is so disturbing I can’t even wrap my mind around it. But the one person she lets know she’s still alive? Anthony! If I had been Emily, John, Amber and Harry, I would have wiped my hands of Claire the moment she decided to go back to Anthony and cut off any and all contact with her. The first time she didn’t have a choice. This time, she <i>chose</i> to go back. He might have initially blackmailed her to go back to him, but she had resources, she had family, she had friends. All these things would have helped her fight Anthony, but Claire didn’t want to fight. She wanted to go back and she wanted to be with him. It’s all on her what happens next!<br /><br /><b>
  <i> The Wrap Up:</i>
</b><br />Needless to say, this is NOT a book I will ever read again. I am permanently deleting it from my Nook and will NOT read book three. I have no desire to read any more of this story or these characters and suffer the frustration it causes. <br /><br /><i>Special Thanks…</i><br />I would like to thank my good friend Juls for reading this and <i>Consequences</i> with me. She kept me sane as we tried to analyze, figure out and come up with reasons why things were happening. And finally, she was there when we both decided to just give up and read the last 90 pages as a free-for-all because we just wanted to get this stupid, messed up story done and over with. Thanks girl.. I’m still completely “Team Kill Evil Anthony” and not even him saving babies in Africa could change my mind! :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13426408308883896962" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_584135176" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/584135176" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/584135176?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16125817-truth">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer584135176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5374362531784893120">While the 'Consequences' series is one of my all-time favorite series, 'Truth' is my absolute favorite book in the series. That isn't to say that all of the books in this series aren't wonderful -- they are. However, this book is so damn great that I can't even begin to express how much I love it. <br/><br/>I frequently find myself returning to this book and rereading my favorite parts. I'm a glutton for punishment that way. Never has a story made me feel more conflicted...or more addicted, than the story</span>
  <span id="freeText5374362531784893120" style="display:none">While the 'Consequences' series is one of my all-time favorite series, 'Truth' is my absolute favorite book in the series. That isn't to say that all of the books in this series aren't wonderful -- they are. However, this book is so damn great that I can't even begin to express how much I love it. <br /><br />I frequently find myself returning to this book and rereading my favorite parts. I'm a glutton for punishment that way. Never has a story made me feel more conflicted...or more addicted, than the story of Tony and Claire. I just cannot get enough of this screwed up, controversial and suspenseful story. <br /><br />After the huge upset at the end of 'Consequences', it is no surprise that 'Truth' takes Claire and Tony's story in a new direction. So much has changed. Yet, so much remains the same.<br /><br />While many of Claire's actions continue to be irrational and perplexing, I am so glad that Aleatha Romig dreamed up her character. Otherwise, I would have never experienced this phenomenal story. While all rational thought should send Claire running as far away from Tony as she can get, I'm so glad that she continues to defy all reason and repeatedly engages in his games. I cannot get enough of it!<br /><br />In comparison to her demeanor in 'Consequences', 'Truth' shows a more independent and strong-minded version of Claire. She is no longer trapped at Tony's mansion, at the mercy of his violent whims. This book sees Claire pursue more of an "offensive" approach to her interactions with Tony, whereas Claire had previously been limited to a sort of passive resistance. <br /><br />Nevertheless, Tony is not one to be out-maneuvered. Time and time again, he proves that he is still in control. The back and forth antics of Tony and Claire keeps me flipping the pages every time I read this book. <br /><br />Even though I should hate Tony, I just can't. That is the beauty of this series. In fact, as "truths" are revealed and more of his horrendous actions come to light, I find myself trying to fight a stronger pull to him. He is the epitome of an anti-hero. I love him more, despite all reason, with each new detail shared. I can relate to Claire in that regard. <br /><br />This second book in the series begins a slow unveiling of Tony's motivations. Little by little, Claire begins to unearth details of a their families' shared past. The depth of Tony's hunger for revenge is astounding. Claire tries to gather clues to figure out exactly where she fits into the picture. <br /><br />This book was jam-packed with information. Blink and you'll miss something. Each time I read it, I pick up on something else that I overlooked before. <br /><br />Not only are "truths" revealed in this book, but new mysteries surface. For every question answered, more questions arise. I was on the edge of my seat the entire time.<br /><br />Once again, Claire finds herself in danger. Only this time, the person trying to harm her is unknown. Is Tony really trying to turn over a new leaf or is he up to his old tricks? Can Claire ever trust him after everything that he's done? Is there somebody else that wants to do her harm?<br /><br />In addition to all of the facts that are unveiled in this book, the introduction of several new characters makes for a multi-dimensional story. Claire finds an unlikely friend in Amber, the fiancée of her recently deceased ex-boyfriend. Amber's brother, Harry, also plays a pivotal role in this book, helping Claire adjust to her new life. Phil, a private investigator hired by Tony, also ends up being a key player this time around. The introduction of Derek and Sophia Burke adds yet another layer to this story, while familiar characters like Courtney and Brent evolve further.<br /><br />I don't want to give too much away, as I believe that this series should be experienced. I cannot begin to coherently state how much I love this series, or why. It is simply spectacular! <br /><br />If you like darker reads, full of suspense, romance and mystery, then this is one is a must-read. You have to go into it with an open mind though. This story is not for those with "triggers" related to abuse, etc. It is full of controversial, offensive subject matter. However, if you love stories that mess with your head and make you step outside of your comfort zone, then you don't want to miss it.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5374362531784893120" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_449821133" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449821133" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/449821133?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449821133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7542405544986888534"><br/><b>And the game continues.....</b><br/><br/><i>Actions and their consequences are just one side of a coin.The side which receives light.<br/><br/>On the other side,lying in the shadows is the <b>...TRUTH behind those actions which resulted in those CONSEQUENCES.</b></i><br/><br/>By the end of the first book we saw how Anthony Rawlings(Tony),the utterly cruel,conniving and manipulative devil played the game to perfection.He had his vengeance.<b>And it appeared that as his last move,he disclosed all his pieces to Claire.</b> <br/><br/>At last everything was clear.</span>
  <span id="freeText7542405544986888534" style="display:none"><br /><b>And the game continues.....</b><br /><br /><i>Actions and their consequences are just one side of a coin.The side which receives light.<br /><br />On the other side,lying in the shadows is the <b>...TRUTH behind those actions which resulted in those CONSEQUENCES.</b></i><br /><br />By the end of the first book we saw how Anthony Rawlings(Tony),the utterly cruel,conniving and manipulative devil played the game to perfection.He had his vengeance.<b>And it appeared that as his last move,he disclosed all his pieces to Claire.</b> <br /><br />At last everything was clear.<br /><br />But.....***shakes head***<br /><br /><br />When am I going to learn? <b>APPEARANCES!!!<br /><br />Appearances deceive.Nothing is as it seems.</b><br /><br />In the last book,we saw the thousand and one facades of Anthony and even Claire.<br /><br />In this book the <b>masks will be ripped off</b> and the people behind those masks will be revealed.<br /><br /><i>Is the dark persona of Anthony real or is it just a mask or is it a bit of both?<br /><br />Is Claire the quiet,meek submissive or under all that lies a core of steel?</i><br /><br />The questions are answered here and more...<br /><br />Some new (pieces)characters are introduced in this book too.Each has his/her own role to play.<br /><br /><b>The game is still on,but the stakes are even higher...<br /><br />Anthony and Claire will have to decide whether they will be playing against each other or have to unite their forces to thwart an UNSEEN ENEMY,whom none of them has ever anticipated.<br /><br />An enemy more cruel,more ruthless and more evil!!An enemy who is driven by a lust for vengeance more stronger than even Anthony's.An enemy who doesn't have his/her own personal beacon of light,as Claire is Anthony's.<br /><br /><br />Would-be-readers of this book,get ready...hang on tight....or you'll be sucked inside the vortex which is TRUTH.</b><br /><br /><br />Short storyline--<br /><br />After 18 months of serving her sentence,Claire is pardoned.Which means that her every record of committing the (framed) crime has been wiped off.Amazed,she tries to build a new life in California with Amber,the fiancee of deceased Simon.She meets with Harry,Amber's brother.She reconnects with her sister Emily.All the time hoping that Tony doesn't find her.<br /><br />Tony get's word of her release after two weeks(the news was kept under wraps). Tony is furious.He seeks Claire out.Well,if you are thinking that it was because of his unfulfilled vengeance,then you are wrong...<br /><br />Why? Please read the book.I do not want to spoil the shocks you'll get,one after the other.<br /><br /><br />But,I had hoped that Tony would face the consequences of his actions,and he did........<br /><br /><b>"I'm so sorry...for everything... why? ...why did you leave me?"As the tears coated his cheeks he told himself,<i>Anthony Rawlings doesn't cry.He doesn't apologize,and he doesn't cry...</i></b><br /><br />Though my heart cried a little too.<br /><br />For those who think I'm crazy,you try and read this book and not fall for him.<br /><br /><b>Why are you still listening to my babble,(or reading shall I say)???Go and grab the book.Right now!!!</b><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_459246851" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/459246851" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/459246851?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer459246851" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6902606210790630894"><b>Some of the emotions I felt while reading this book...</b><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769177.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769178.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769179.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769180.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769181.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769182.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><br/>Just like <i>Consequences</i>, the first part of this highly enticing, fascinating and mind-boggling series, <i>Truth</i> (again) left me speechless, shocked and just emotionally exhausted after finishing it. It also left me in awe of the amazing writer that is Aleatha Romig, for creating such a marvelous story that can make you feel so many emotions during such a short period of time.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>After you've dealt with the Consequences, pre</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText6902606210790630894" style="display:none"><b>Some of the emotions I felt while reading this book...</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769177.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769178.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769179.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769180.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769181.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398145ra/769182.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>Just like <i>Consequences</i>, the first part of this highly enticing, fascinating and mind-boggling series, <i>Truth</i> (again) left me speechless, shocked and just emotionally exhausted after finishing it. It also left me in awe of the amazing writer that is Aleatha Romig, for creating such a marvelous story that can make you feel so many emotions during such a short period of time.<br><br><b>
  <i>After you've dealt with the Consequences, prepare yourself to face <u>the Truth</u>...</i>
</b><br><br>What happened in <i>Consequences</i> was only the beginning, what follows in <i>Truth</i> is the unravelling of a masterfully created web of secrets and deceits that will most of the time leave you on the edge of your seat.<br><br>When Claire is released from prison after being incarcerated for 18 months, she hopes to finally move on with her life, her life <b>without Tony</b>. She moves to California to live with her newfound friend and ally Amber (fiancee of Claire's deceased former boyfriend Simon) and her brother Harry. But, as to be expected, Tony isn't ready to let Claire go that easily, he hunts her down and what follows is an emotional and psychological figurative game of chess that will, in the end, lead us to the <i>Truth</i>... <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Perhaps, someday she'd learn to expect the unexpected, and his actions wouldn't shock her. Yet, as was their history, whenever Anthony Rawlings was in Claire's life, so was the potential for abrupt change."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>In this second part there are some very interesting new characters and although the story no longer solely takes part around the close surroundings of the Rawlings' Mansion; in the end it all comes down to this: <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>Same game,<br><br>Same rules,<br><br>Same main players.</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's like chess. I make a move, he makes a move. Eventually one of us will declare <u>check-mate</u>."<br><br>"From my short experience, I believe you're a worthy opponent."<br><br>"You see, that's where I'm confused. Sometimes I think I'm an opponent. Other times I think he believes I'm the prize."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398145i/769183.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"In their figurative game of chess, Anthony Rawlings had Claire <u>in check</u>. Every move she made, he countered."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398145i/769184.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Of all the animals, man is the only one that is cruel. He is the only one that inflicts pain for the pleasure of doing it." ~ Mark Twain</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br> <br>In this "game" nothing is as it seems and just when you think you've figured it out, something unexpected happens and you are left in the dark once again to ponder on what the meaning of everything you've just read, is. <br><br>As for Tony, I have to admit, as much as I hated and detested the man that is Anthony Rawlings in <i>Consequences</i>; in <i>Truth</i> we do get to see a much different side of him. We learn about his history and everything he's been through in his young life. And we learn that there is in fact a more human, lighthearted side to him that might make you want to revise your entire opinion about him. But, nonetheless, the man has a lot of issues and my main message to him would still be: <br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/424457.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>Overall, this series is a definite <u>MUST-READ!!!</u> I would highly recommend reading it to everyone and to embark on this extremely entertaining (to say the least) roller coaster ride, a ride that will propably stay with you for a very long time after you're finished with it...<br><br><b>Well done, Aleatha Romig, well done!!<br></b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/411750.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><i>And now I <u>can't wait</u> to read <b>Convicted</b> and find out what will happen in the next part of this unbelievable story...</i><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1967293558" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1967293558" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1967293558?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1967293558" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5623964835592488966"><b>Fool me once, shame on you; fool me twice, shame on me</b><br/><br/>If the first book was the perfect nightmare, the second book is the perfect fairytale. <br/><br/>So Claire will have a second chance for happiness. <br/>Finally free from jail, free from Tony, free from debts; she will be surrounded with old and new friends, her family, new allies and a new boyfriend.<br/><br/>Tony definitely will not like losing control of Claire and her life. He has never wanted to let her go.<br/><br/>But what about Claire? Surely she should be happy. But s</span>
  <span id="freeText5623964835592488966" style="display:none"><b>Fool me once, shame on you; fool me twice, shame on me</b><br /><br />If the first book was the perfect nightmare, the second book is the perfect fairytale. <br /><br />So Claire will have a second chance for happiness. <br />Finally free from jail, free from Tony, free from debts; she will be surrounded with old and new friends, her family, new allies and a new boyfriend.<br /><br />Tony definitely will not like losing control of Claire and her life. He has never wanted to let her go.<br /><br />But what about Claire? Surely she should be happy. But something is missing. <br />Maybe deep down Claire never wanted to be free.<br /><br />Claire apparently does not like taking decisions. She prefers it when someone chooses her clothes and her food at the restaurant. Her new boyfriend gives her the freedom of choice. He always asks her opinion. But maybe Claire is well trained by Tony. She is the perfect submissive. She can only take what she is given. She does not ask.<br /><br />Tony….the rapist, the sadist, the possibly killer, the respectable businessman, the shark. I tried very hard to understand him, but I gave up. <br /><br />Tony and Claire’s love is twisted. Not many of the people that they really know them understand it. But that is okay in the fiction world. <br /><br />Some may say that Claire when she gets a normal boyfriend, she also gets a new chance in love. <br />It just looks as a distraction to me. A way to postpone the inevitable. Not a really important relationship, because Claire undoubtedly craves the dominance of Tony.<br /><br /><u>There are different kinds of monsters and devils in this world. If the “victim” agrees to her torture, then she is not a victim. And if the “tormentor” is accepted, then he is not really a tormentor. </u><br /><br />Claire is a perfect match for Tony. I wouldn’t take him, but this is her life.<br /><br />What I did not like in the book:<br />-Still there is PP (product placement). At least this time is less extensive in comparison to Consequences. Reading about all these brands that I cannot afford can be very painful LOL. <br />-While “Consequences” was an extremely slow book; “Truth” is a bit too fast in some instances that I want it to be really slow. When good things are happening I really want to savor them. I want to appreciated them and learn all the details. Especially towards the end, when Claire is winning battles. I want to know everything. Instead I get a perfect moment fast-forward in a perfect isolated tropical island in the future, where I need to speculate the facts and imagine the most important scene of the book.<br /><br />I was not bored with this book. There are many twists and many surprises. There is also another mastermind more ruthless, psychotic and devilish than Tony. <br /><br />Additionally, the moments that Tony is trying really hard not to be such a frighteningly controlling, manipulated bastard are really satisfying and amusing.<br /><br />------------------------<br />------------------------<br />BEFORE STARTING THE BOOK<br /><br />Before I start the next book of the series, I just wish that toxic acid rain will fall on Tony Rawlings while he is sunbathing.<br />And consequently he will die a horrible death.<br />And his ashes will be scattered in North, East, West and South with the help of at least 6 different types of winds. <br />While black crows will laugh at him.<br />And nobody will remember him ever again on the face of the earth.<br /><br />This is the book that supposedly will make me change my opinion about him. HA HA.<br />Bring it on!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5623964835592488966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer434655190" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10481546352933329362"><b>Spoiler Free Review</b> -Quick review<br/>4.5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: Adult Fiction -Psychological Thriller<br/><br/><b>ARE YOU READY FOR THE TRUTH???</b> I sure as hell wasn't....<br/><b>NOTHING</b>, absolutely<b> NOTHING</b> was what it appeared to be, yet<b> EVERYTHING</b> weaved together flawlessly with a<b> JAW DROPPER</b> ending.<br/><br/><b>In Consequences</b><br/><i>A man with no compassion started to feel compassion.<br/>A man with no regrets started to regret.<br/>A man who NEVER apologizes, apologized.<br/>Claire's ability to ADAPT produced CHANGE.<br/>Claire's decision to adapt provided h</i></span>
  <span id="freeText10481546352933329362" style="display:none"><b>Spoiler Free Review</b> -Quick review<br />4.5 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Adult Fiction -Psychological Thriller<br /><br /><b>ARE YOU READY FOR THE TRUTH???</b> I sure as hell wasn't....<br /><b>NOTHING</b>, absolutely<b> NOTHING</b> was what it appeared to be, yet<b> EVERYTHING</b> weaved together flawlessly with a<b> JAW DROPPER</b> ending.<br /><br /><b>In Consequences</b><br /><i>A man with no compassion started to feel compassion.<br />A man with no regrets started to regret.<br />A man who NEVER apologizes, apologized.<br />Claire's ability to ADAPT produced CHANGE.<br />Claire's decision to adapt provided her with a wealth of knowledge. She has learned from the master and now she can use it to her advantage.</i><br /> <br /><br /><b>Freedom</b><br />In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070018.Truth__Consequences___2_" title="Truth (Consequences, #2) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Truth</a> Claire is released from prison after doing an eighteen month stint. Shocked yet grateful she seeks solace in sunny California with an unexpected friend. But happy day's of freedom don't last forever because when Tony get's word of her release....Well....Let's just say he is none to pleased. His unhappiness however does not stem from her newly found freedom but from his loss of control. AND the fact that he still wants her. Which is something he never anticipated.<br /><br />A new game begins with a host of new players. Unbeknownst to him, puppet master Tony is no longer pulling the strings. Because there is someone more <b>EVIL</b> lurking around to take out both him and Claire. And the new puppet master is ten times colder, twenty times more calculated and very much determined to win.<br /><br />Truth takes off with a BOOM and keeps up the momentum at high rate speed; with it's perfectly spun web of events that are mind consuming. Romig has crafted a well developed plot, strong characters and jaw dropping story lines. This book kept me on the edge of my seat the whole time as the truth was slowly revealed piece by piece. I consider this series A MUST READ! You will not be disappointed!<br /><br />My ratings<br />Characters- Cunning <br />Writing Style- Methodical, Leading and Skillful<br />Plot/Storyline- Clever, Deceptive, and Intense<br />Steam Factor- Medium/Moderately Steamy<br />Overall- I loved it!!<b> A MUST READ!!</b><br /><b><br />Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b></span>

</a><br/><br/>Wow , If <i>Consequences</i> was all about actions and cons</span>
  <span id="freeText8223015668320990666" style="display:none"><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/oh%20my%20god%20gif/AlucardFangirl/Animated%20GIFs/omg.gif?o=10" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375450ra/730021.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/oh%20my%20god%20gif/idril_earfalas/Gif/tumblr_m0iax954bI1r7zpqd.gif?o=5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763313.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> 10,000+ truthfully gleaming stars !!!! </b><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/angst%20gif/fruzs/tumblr_lmq2wna4jJ1qgzqnco1_500.gif?o=6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763314.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Give me <b>CONVICTED</b> like right now !!!!! <br><br><b> EDIT : 11/05/2012 </b><br><br><b>
  <i> Things are not always what they seem; the first appearance deceives many. The intelligence of a few, perceives what has been carefully hidden — Roman poet Phaedrus </i>
</b><br><br><b> SUPERCALIFRAGILISTICEXPIALIDOCIOUS !!!!! </b><br><br>I'm spent ! Exhausted ! Both Mentally and Emotionally ! <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/tired%20gif/uvbeenpotod/sleep.gif?o=12" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763315.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mrs Aleatha Romig , you deserve a standing ovation for sure ...<br><br><a href="http://s636.photobucket.com/albums/uu90/vanessa68_2009/Macros%20and%20gifs/?action=view&amp;current=1078584.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763316.gif" alt="Applause Standing Ovation" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Wow , If <i>Consequences</i> was all about actions and consequences , then <i> Truth </i> is all about the truth that had paved the way to those actions . Infact , its all about separating the lies and deceptions from the truth . Honestly speaking , I'm not going to get into what this book is going to offer story wise because there is no way I can do that without giving away a lot of spoilers . And its something I dont want to do . This journey is for the reader and for the reader alone . The blurb gives a perfect description of what you will be getting yourself into ... okay , maybe not <b> EXACTLY </b> what you'll be getting into , but if you've read the first book then there shouldn't be a question of thinking what you can expect from this book . Aleatha is a mastermind-ish twister of events , scenes and scenario's ! <i> Phew ... that was exhausting ! </i><br><br>All I'll say now is that you have to abandon most of your assumptions because like the fact that is mentioned above , <b> NOTHING IS AS IT SEEMS ! AND THE TRUTH SHALL SET YOU FREE FROM THE LIES ! </b> .. In a way it would , but then it'll probably ground you back with a dozen new questions . <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/trustme/ladiepandora/trustme-1.jpg?o=13" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396127i/763317.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Consequences ended with a lot of explosions ! But that wasn't the end of it . In Truth , Claire tries to find out more about the man that is Anthony Rawlings . His past and what makes him what he is . We definitely got a bit of his history in Consequences but that was just a small part of a much bigger picture . <br><br>I loved Claire in this book . Her decisions were a bit shocking at times , but thats just who she is , or thats what she's made up of . Somehow , I found her as a person who looks into the soul of a Person . Someone who is optimistic in her approach towards life . And judging by that there was no questioning the path she took . But is she right or wrong ? She was a victim before , but this time , has she deliberately walked into a trap that could lead her to darkness ? Or has she bought about a change that no one expected ? A change of heart and mind . A change of Priority . Only time will tell . <br><br>Tony ... All I can say is , " Oh my god , was he for realz ?? " He is still manipulative , he is still controlling but .. but ... he just stole by heart . Sexy as hell and mighty fine I tell ya . He has a little humorous side to him too . God , how much I loved him here in spite of all the douchery that he was in book 1 . I'm not saying thats forgettable but he's only human so ..... yeah I sound a bit biased here but .... <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=I-Love-Him-So-Much.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763318.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There I said it ... <br><br>The ending !!!!! God lord , that ending was just <br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/mind%20blown%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380369097ra/721781.gif" alt="Mind Blown Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I shouldn't even be surprised , this is Aleatha Romig we are talking about . But still .... speechless !<br><br>Aleatha Romig really knows how to have her way with words. If Consequences had a very eerie and a dread like feel to it , then truth was all about anticipation and surprises . I'm sure you must have noticed that every chapter begins with a quote , and somehow I felt that those quotes are so rightly placed because they end up giving a feel or what that chapter is all about . She very cleverly creates a web of words and actions that leaves the reader all tangled up . It took me two days to write up this review , because every time I thought about the book , I ended up seeing things in different shades . That ending ... just AWESOME ! <br><br>This is such a Hollywood movie material . Its a perfect mixture of :<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_mcz2b9n5bi1rgb4bxo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763319.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>a little action , a hint of humor , a lot of mystery and a huge dose of suspense ! <br><br>To sum up the entire review , Truth is a journey from darkness to light , from the unknown to the known , from the expected to the unexpected .. <i> yup you read that right </i> . From assumptions to reality . <br><br>I'm definitely going to be on pins and needles till Convicted come out !! <br><br>Oh , before I go , Aleatha , Failure to give me a HEA is not an option . Any other conclusion to this series is non-negotiable and undebatable . Do not disappoint me . <a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/wink%20gif/kingphilip2/wink.gif?o=6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396127ra/763320.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br></span>

I hated that she didn't talk about her days in prison.When she was confronting him, she would bring all the stupid shit like how he broke her little heart and how she trusted him and why he divorced her.But NEVER did she mentioned how could he sent her and James in jail,how much Emily suffered.She own it to them to be angry at him.<br><br> overall I was bored with all the designer labels and shopping and galas. I know some people consider this to be one of those mindfuck books but I just find it infuriating and keep waiting to click with any character and actually care about what happens to them.</span>

  <i>The Police in a press conference, shared today new information regarding the recent murder of a Kindle Keyboard that has shocked the reading community. Police officials have confirmed that the suspicions about the authenticity of the note, pointing the world renowned bussinessman Anthony Rawlings as the main suspect, is in question. The investigation is considered ongoing and there weren't made any other comments. Our reporters are trying since, to contact Mr. Rawlings but he is unreachable. </i></p></span>
  <span id="freeText12050900586802903628" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397860i/768127.gif" width="343" height="62" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>
  <i>The Police in a press conference, shared today new information regarding the recent murder of a Kindle Keyboard that has shocked the reading community. Police officials have confirmed that the suspicions about the authenticity of the note, pointing the world renowned bussinessman Anthony Rawlings as the main suspect, is in question. The investigation is considered ongoing and there weren't made any other comments. Our reporters are trying since, to contact Mr. Rawlings but he is unreachable. We will continue to keep you informed as new evidence surface...</i>
</p><br><br><b>5+++ AMAZING STARS</b><br>Another winner for Aleatha Romig and in my opinion even better than the first book!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397860ra/768128.gif" width="350" height="197" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was stunned, I was speechless and by the end I was breathless. This book grabbed me and never let me go and my GOD what a ride! If I have to find a minor minus, I'll say that the parts about Sophia started as intriguing but until her importance in the story was revealed they were a little boring, only because I was bitting my nails to found out more about Tony (yeah in this book he is definitely a Tony!) and Claire. The title is Truth and the book does live up to its title. We learn the whole truth and the heroes face it no matter the consequences...<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397860i/768129.jpg" width="411" height="486" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>These book are a chess game. A game that is being played for about 30 years. Every move has a significance and its piece equal importance, because let's not forget: a pawn that reaches its eighth rank (a row of the chessboard) can be transformed into the player's choice of a queen, knight, rook, or bishop. So don't underestimate anyone! (All of us did it...) <br><br><i>Out of suffering have emerged the strongest souls;<br>the most massive characters are seared with scars.</i><br>- Kahlil Gibran as quoted by Aleatha Romig<br><br><b>Anthony Rawlings:</b> In this book he not only shows redeeming qualities, he managed to throw away his stoic mask and give us a glimpse of the vulnerable man who hides. I finally saw that he trully loves Claire and his love may be obsessive and possesive but is also deep and everlasting... I don't forgive him his atrocious actions, I just see a way to put them in the past and start anew.<br><br><b>Claire Nichols:</b> Well, she still is a little doormat-y for my taste. She is impulsive and immature, indecisive and naive. In the end she managed to surprise me and in an epic twist, just I was ready to destroy my Kindle, she moved for the win and eventually after two whole books I cheered for her!!! Claire your final plan ROCKED!!!!!!!<br><br>Saying all that doesn't mean I condone or even understand the actions of these people. I still find myself an innocent bystander, willing but unable to stop the proverbial train wreck. <br><br>Now, I'm more than ready for book #3... I seriously can't wait to get my hands on it. The questions are finally semi-answered, all the pieces are set and the last moves will decide the WINNER. <br>So, let me check the release date..<br>.<br>.<br>.<br>WHAT?<br><i>WHAT?</i><br><b>
  <i>WHAT?</i>
</b><br><b>
  <i>2013? And possibly mid to late 2013?</i>

If you have added them but for some reason you haven't started them yet, stop waisting time!! A MUST READ!</b><br> </span>
