<div id="review_478916126" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478916126" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478916126?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=lost-love-rekindled">lost-love-rekindled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=non-con">non-con</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478916126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12513585214273853753">This is, quite simply, a brilliantly told mind-bender.<br/><br/>If Consequences was a jigsaw with pieces missing, then Truth is most definitely a strategic game of chess.<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401056i/777810.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I think it’s nigh on impossible to review without giving away too many plotlines which no reader should know before embarking on this one. I want you to go in blind, the way I did – I want you to feel what I did. I lost sleep over these books, I never knew what was coming next, Aleatha Romig has the ability to constantly surprise and </span>
  <span id="freeText12513585214273853753" style="display:none">This is, quite simply, a brilliantly told mind-bender.<br><br>If Consequences was a jigsaw with pieces missing, then Truth is most definitely a strategic game of chess.<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401056i/777810.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think it’s nigh on impossible to review without giving away too many plotlines which no reader should know before embarking on this one. I want you to go in blind, the way I did – I want you to feel what I did. I lost sleep over these books, I never knew what was coming next, Aleatha Romig has the ability to constantly surprise and she wields this weapon over us readers with, I suspect, wicked glee!! What is going on here is just plain, good old-fashioned story telling. It’s an incredibly well-crafted story with layers constantly peeling back to reveal yet more shocking truths. <br><br>As a reader, I felt like I constantly teetered on the edge of an abyss of obsession, madness, hidden identities and vengeance and, even after so many Truths were revealed, it remains a compelling mystery that I still can’t quite unravel. Thankfully, there is to be a third book, Convicted, to finally tie up all the loose ends and, once and for all, finally explain who exactly did what and why they did it. The whole book is incredibly compelling and a worthy sequel to Consequences, a book which left me completely stunned by the turn of events. It’s enigmatic, tense and never deviates from the central emotional quandary – can Claire ever forgive Tony for his actions? Can anything justify what he has done to Claire and those who love her?<br><br>I will say that, for me, Tony was 100% villain by the end of Consequences. I could never have envisioned finding a happy place for him in my imagination but Aleatha Romig is an absolute mistress of misdirection and she has bent my mind once again and now I find I have sympathy and even empathy for him. By the end of Truth, I feel now that I understand him and his motivations better. I still really do not like what he did and I need to hear more about that fateful day from his perspective but Tony and I now have an entente-cordiale and a fragile peace exists between us.<br><br>Claire – after being such a victim for nearly all of the first book, has now grown a backbone of steel. She’s been bitchslapped by the last three years of her life into a much stronger and resolute woman and she now knows what she wants, what she wants to avenge and how she is going to go about it. I did feel for a while that she dallied a little with other people’s affections and kindness but, for the most part, there’s a lot to admire in her in this book.<br><br>There’s also the addition of several very important secondary characters who have a big role to play in what happens here and also startling revelations about established characters although I will confess I worked out the ‘biggie’, fairly early on in this one through the frequent flash-backs and flash-sideways. Truth gets off to a fairly explosive beginning and then stalls to a fairly sedate pace before once again picking up speed and galloping for the finish line. It’s absolutely unputdownable. Is that a word? Well, whatever, it describes it perfectly.<br><br>This was another 5 star review for me but it’s almost impossible to classify. I labelled Consequences as ‘dark-non-con’ and I guess it falls under that category for the darkness but there’s also contemporary romance and suspense going on here too. This is a fantastic series – I am going to highly recommend it.<br><br>Series Reading Order<br><br>1.Consequences<br>2. Truth - released Nov 2012<br>3. Convicted - release expected 2013: date tbc<br><br><i>Review copy courtesy of Aleatha Romig<br><br>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a></i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12513585214273853753" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag"><img alt="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410910791p2/8191340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940015928396" href="/book/show/16098096-truth">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=mind-f-k">mind-f-k</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=psych-thriller">psych-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer430612739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5259037102540883517">“It was amazing how the mind can twist things, making them legitimate, especially under duress.”<br/><br/> Bravo, Aleatha Romig for exceeding my expectations with a second book in a series.<br/><br/> <b>It was mindfuckingly-beautiful!</b> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393760ra/758186.gif' width='250' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The twists and turns, screams and yearning- all so well done. After Consequences, I had a plan for Claire to be strong and take “the man” DOWN… but oh no, you had other plans for us and I believe the story (the game) is just going to be better played. <br/>Ms. Romig, you make me want to pick </span>
  <span id="freeText5259037102540883517" style="display:none">“It was amazing how the mind can twist things, making them legitimate, especially under duress.”<br><br> Bravo, Aleatha Romig for exceeding my expectations with a second book in a series.<br><br> <b>It was mindfuckingly-beautiful!</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393760ra/758186.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The twists and turns, screams and yearning- all so well done. After Consequences, I had a plan for Claire to be strong and take “the man” DOWN… but oh no, you had other plans for us and I believe the story (the game) is just going to be better played. <br>Ms. Romig, you make me want to pick up every thought-provoking psychological thriller book and devour it. You wreaked havoc with my mind and emotions and I hated it but yet want more of it. <br><br><b>I still may be in this camp:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393760i/758187.jpg" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>However, I soon may be buying a new shirt:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393760i/758188.jpg" width="150" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>...and I cannot wait until the third book when all will be solved and resolved and I can stop saying this:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380349365ra/703367.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer463403258" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2450057066794835719"><b>5 Mind Blowing I Will Never Be The Same Again after Reading This Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381100895i/4199875._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>There was no question in his mind— he’d seriously underestimated this woman.</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381100895i/4199876._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>Mr. Anthony Rawlings had a lesson to learn, and this time Claire claimed the role as teacher.</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381103678i/4209392.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let me start out by saying that I hated...no that's not right. I despised...no, that's not quite accurate. I LOATHED Tony in Consequences. I kept asking myself how in the fuck people could be team Tony with such a cruel, brutal, and in my eyes irredeema</span>
  <span id="freeText2450057066794835719" style="display:none"><b>5 Mind Blowing I Will Never Be The Same Again after Reading This Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381100895i/4199875._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>There was no question in his mind— he’d seriously underestimated this woman.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381100895i/4199876._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>Mr. Anthony Rawlings had a lesson to learn, and this time Claire claimed the role as teacher.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381103678i/4209392.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me start out by saying that I hated...no that's not right. I despised...no, that's not quite accurate. I LOATHED Tony in Consequences. I kept asking myself how in the fuck people could be team Tony with such a cruel, brutal, and in my eyes irredeemable asshole. <i>(Now I should probably admit that my internal masochist was silently hoping that he would redeem himself. That bitch is eternally optimistic and has a thing for irredeemable assholes. I just didn't think it was possible with Tony.)</i><br><br>So imagine my surprise where halfway through this book I not only began to feel for him, and actually (gasp) like him, but became a full fledged member of team fucking Tony.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381251479ra/4597877.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book fucked with my head. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381103678i/4209392.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Claire once read that time doesn't pass at normal speeds within a black hole. If one were to travel into a black hole for only moments and return again, centuries would have passed. That explained the sensation she felt, once again peering into his dark gaze.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381251901ra/4598467.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Tony was a giant magnet. His pull affected everything, from the rotation of the earth, to her mind’s ability to reason.</i>
  </b>
  <br>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381252346ra/4599131.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh Claire, I feel for you. I was right there with you. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381103678i/4209392.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm not even sure how to go about reviewing this book without revealing any spoilers. So I'm not even going to try. I was questioning where Aleatha Romig would take this series. I struggled through some parts of Consequences. It was one tough fucking pill to swallow. This book? I have one thing to say to you, Ms. Romig<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421628ra/837783.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I forever worship at the altar of your greatness.<br><br>Holy shit. I'm speechless. My mind? Blown! My sanity? Well what little of it was left...gone! I will never be the same. Truth was a crazy thrill ride filled with enough twists and turns to keep you on the edge of your seat until the very last page. And then when you read the end?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381253096ra/4599803.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book will keep you guessing until the end, it will make you question EVERYTHING and you will still not be close to what the truth is. I couldn't put it down. My brain hurt. I was going crazy. I needed a shot or 5 of vodka once I finished. But FUCK! What a ride!<br><br><i>Luckily I had reinforcement, because I'm pretty sure...no, I KNOW, I would not have been able to handle this ride alone. <br><br>P.S. What a way to pop your BR cherry than with this series, Mirjana &lt;3 AHAHAHAHAHA!!!</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1521327-mirjana-and-lkay-s-truth-br-and-kumbaya-circle" rel="nofollow noopener">https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1521327-mirjana-and-lkay-s-truth-br-and-kumbaya-circle</a><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></span>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/461877628?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer461877628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14773545318515831562"><b>
  <i> “All truths are easy to understand once they are discovered. The trick is to discover them.” -Gallolao </i>
</b> <br/><br/>Okay, seriously, my mind has just been blown!!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/new%20girl%20gif/cheesegirl33/GIF/GIF%20New%20Girl/whaaaaaat.gif?o=7' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398538ra/770387.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Yeah... thats how I feel. I am shocked by that ending. Did not see that coming at all! And I have to wait how long to find out what happens next?!?!?!?!? Late 2013/Early 2014- Are you kidding me????<br/><br/>I’m not gonna lie- I wasn't 100% sure how I felt about Consequences, but this book was <b>phenomenal</b> It was long, but it kept me on my toes the </span>
  <span id="freeText14773545318515831562" style="display:none"><b>
  <i> “All truths are easy to understand once they are discovered. The trick is to discover them.” -Gallolao </i>
</b> <br><br>Okay, seriously, my mind has just been blown!!!!<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/new%20girl%20gif/cheesegirl33/GIF/GIF%20New%20Girl/whaaaaaat.gif?o=7" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398538ra/770387.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yeah... thats how I feel. I am shocked by that ending. Did not see that coming at all! And I have to wait how long to find out what happens next?!?!?!?!? Late 2013/Early 2014- Are you kidding me????<br><br>I’m not gonna lie- I wasn't 100% sure how I felt about Consequences, but this book was <b>phenomenal</b> It was long, but it kept me on my toes the entire time. Just when I thought I had everything figured out- BAM- I was totally wrong. <br><br><i>
  <b> “I think it was a game to both of you, a real life chess game. Every move you made he countered. In order to get his king, you sacrificed your queen, a bold move. One I believe will work. But at what cost?” </b>
</i><br><br><b>Claire-</b> as usual, infuriated me a lot of this book. Although she did have much more of a backbone at times- especially the beginning. She was much stronger than I gave her credit for. <br> <b>Anthony/Tony/Anton</b>- I hated Tony for much of this book. He was still obsessive, crazy, creepy, and totally out of control. But then, I didn’t so much. I hated my self for not hating him the last 10-15% of the book. I wanted to, I really did. What is wrong with me?!?! So conflicted when it comes to Tony. Tony is the bad guy- why did I start to feel for him?!?!? He is truly messed up and did some unforgivable things- but I feel he is on the road to redemption. It may be wrong, and after hating him so much in Consequences, I feel bad for saying this.... but I am SO TEAM TONY &lt;3 &lt;3 <br><b>Harry and Amber</b>- I seriously loved you both... Especially Harry! I wished things would have worked out for him differently. <br><b>Courtney and Brent</b>- Loved you both even more in this book than the last! Courtney- you are freaking awesome!<br><b>Phil</b>- At first I wasn't sure how I felt about him... but I ended up really enjoying his character. <br><b>Derek and Sophia</b>- I had a lot of theories on you two- I’m glad I was wrong on some accounts. Although<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I assumed early on Sophia was Catherine Marie’s long lost daughter. Now I worry for her safety. I still don’t know if her parents dying was really an ‘accident’ Maybe we will find out in the next book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> They had the most awesome relationship, I hope we see more of them in the next book! <br><b>Catherine</b> One of my favorite characters from Consequences... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Looks like I am THE WORST JUDGE OF CHARACTER EVER!!!! Even when I learned she was Marie, I still thought she was on Claire/Tony’s side. She is soooo vindictive. And awful. Plus- BITCH IS CRAZY! I really want to know whats going to happen in the next book with her. Seriously. I. was. shocked. Never saw it coming!!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>These books are unlike anything I have ever read. They had me all over the place. I still don’t understand what some of these characters were thinking. I felt like as soon as some of my questions were answered, more came about. It never ends! Like I said before, at first I wasn’t too sure how I felt about these books. But I <u>loved</u> Truth! It was <u>brilliant!</u> If you haven’t read this, you are missing out!<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=meli-s-top-favourites">meli-s-top-favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=mind-f-ck">mind-f-ck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=love-hate-relationship">love-hate-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=older-man-younger-woman">older-man-younger-woman</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522329399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15533368177844588294"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 'WOW' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381210517ra/4535036.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"You’re memory is a monster; you forget – it doesn’t. It simply files things away. It keeps things for you, or hides things from you – and summons them to your recall with a will of it’s own. You think you have a memory; but it has you!"<br/><br/>-- John Irving <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Seriously... WOW! This series continues to BLOW my mind. I have no idea how to review this, so if it sucks...</span>
  <span id="freeText15533368177844588294" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 'WOW' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381210517ra/4535036.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You’re memory is a monster; you forget – it doesn’t. It simply files things away. It keeps things for you, or hides things from you – and summons them to your recall with a will of it’s own. You think you have a memory; but it has you!"<br><br>-- John Irving <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Seriously... WOW! This series continues to BLOW my mind. I have no idea how to review this, so if it sucks... sorry.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381206310ra/4525591.gif" width="400" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I started this book with the intention of continuing my hate for Tony and watching Claire get sweet, sweet revenge. So when it begins, I loathe Tony for what he did to Claire. If you read my review of the first book, you know just how much I really hate him. When Claire is liberated from prison, I am so beyond happy that she can finally do something to retaliate. I love that she researches and tries to recreate the mystery box of information she had recieved when she was incarcerated. I love that Claire has Amber and then later on Harry for support. Two people who seem to truly believe in her. And so the ball starts rolling, or should I say, the game of chess begins...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"In their figurative game of chess, Anthony Rawlings had Claire in check. Every move she made, he countered." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381204914i/4522553._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Mr Anthony Rawlings had a lesson to learn and Claire claimed the role as teacher.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>In the beginning, I had so much hope in Claire. I knew she could do it and possibly best Tony in the game. I knew Tony was intelligent, but I felt Claire was often underestimated. Plus I loved the backbone she developed in this one. I liked her interactions with Harry. I really liked him a lot. At one moment I thought he could be really good for her, totally different from what she had with Tony. I also loved that Courtney and Brent were totally supportive of her. Even the hired creeper ended up helping Claire, with some blackmail of course. But it seemed she had all her 'chess pieces' where she needed them to be to carry out her plan. I loved the way she was able to make things go in her favor. Still, there were many moments I was a bit annoyed with Claire for how weak she seemed at times. But like I said, others underestimated her... even I did. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381205612i/4524242._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“This is why I haven’t answered all of your questions. You may think you’re ready for answers, but you’re not. Bits and pieces may help you understand. But, the blatant truth is too much.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh, how I hate Tony. I got so paranoid in the beginning of this book. Whenever something happened, I instantly thought it was him. I was so freaking scared of him. He wouldn't stop stalking claire. Then, I got a upset with her because Tony has a way of getting to her. I was like 'NOOOOO! STAY AWAY FROM HIM! STAY STRONG!' (Yes I may have shouted that at my Kobo. <i>Sorry Kobo</i>) I didn't understand how she could melt for him after ALL he did to her. But she did, and soon the unthinkable happened... I LIKED HIM TOO!! I know!! I was shocked! It didn't happen in one page but still it happened. What is wrong with me?? I have no idea, but Tony turned around. He was 'trying' for her. I will say though, It was really hard for me to accept what he was saying when it came to his feelings. I didn't know if he was playing her again. But I just couldn't help but believe him. He isn't perfect, but he has definitely changed. There was one scene in particular that made me cry for him. I wanted to hug him so bad that's how bad I felt for him. I KNOW! That's crazy! I still don't know how it happened, but I am now on his team. Which really scares the crap out of me. I hope he stays this new Tony for good.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>His glaring abyss penetrated as he demanded, "Say it!"<br><br>Her emerald eyes begged for understanding, uncertain of what he wanted.<br><br>"Say you are mine and nobody else's."<br><br>Her voice resonated above his growl, "Yes, Tony, </i>you<i> are mine and nobody else's." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394801ra/760212.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two new characters were introduced in this book. Derek and Sophia. We were able to get glimpses of Nathaniel's life and how he had a lover, Marie. We were given some new information that finally revealed some of the truth. I knew Derek and Sophia were somehow connected to the past. Almost near the beginning I knew who Sophia would end up being. I ended up being correct. I'm still scared what the future will hold for them. Because it seems someone's revenge is not over and they are now the main targets. I was suspicious of who it was that was behind it all. I had an inkling that is was Marie. But I wasn't sure where she was. After some clues throughout the book, I figured out who and where she was. I couldn't believe Claire hadn't seen it sooner. I was so shocked when I figured it out because I really liked this character. I couldn't believe I was deceived. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I think it was a game to both of you, a real life chess game. Every move you made he countered. In order to get his king, you sacrificed your queen, a bold move. One I believe will work. But at what cost?” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381210336ra/4534700.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending totally STUNNED me. I was not expecting that ending. There were so many twists that messed up with my mind completely. I didn't know what to expect next. I felt all sorts of emotions. I was happy, confused, angry, frustrated, and then more confused. The writing was just brilliant! Absolutely loved the writing and how it was able to keep me enthralled with this story that I didn't want to put it down. I didn't think I would end up liking Tony and I did, no matter how much I resisted. Still, I don't love him... but maybe in book three... we'll see. This book was one crazy ride and I loved every moment of it. I must say, I enjoyed this book better than the first. I still can't believe a character I liked ended up being the biggest evil bitch ever. I can't wait to read the next book. I hope Tony and Claire get their HEA. AND... I hope I get some answers because now I have more questions with that ending. I'm so happy the third installment is out or else the wait would have killed me. An absolute great read. I definitely recommend this book if you don't mind getting mind fucked.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"All truths are easy to understand once they are discovered. The trick is to discover them."<br><br>-- Gallolao <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15533368177844588294" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/490516080?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16125817-truth">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=emotional-reads">emotional-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=action-drama-full-reads">action-drama-full-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=freebies">freebies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=contracts-and-arrangements">contracts-and-arrangements</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=head-fuck">head-fuck</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer490516080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15254855106518681237"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402799i/783146._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402175i/781555._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The only way to possibly start this review is to begin by saying... this book is friggin amazing!!<br/><br/>I loved Consequences, but Truth was just a whole other level! It's definitely going on my favourites shelf, and what a way to start 2013.<br/><br/>I couldn't possibly begin to describe the storyline of Truth. It's so complex, interwoven and mind blowing, that I can't remember what happened in what order. Just know that it is completely gripping.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Mr Anthony Rawlings had a lesson to learn and Claire clai</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15254855106518681237" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402799i/783146._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402175i/781555._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The only way to possibly start this review is to begin by saying... this book is friggin amazing!!<br><br>I loved Consequences, but Truth was just a whole other level! It's definitely going on my favourites shelf, and what a way to start 2013.<br><br>I couldn't possibly begin to describe the storyline of Truth. It's so complex, interwoven and mind blowing, that I can't remember what happened in what order. Just know that it is completely gripping.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Mr Anthony Rawlings had a lesson to learn and Claire claimed the role as teacher.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I read, like the addict I am, every single second I could manage. I was totally addicted to Claire and Tony! And my emotions were all over the place.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>As they sat, him on the sofa and her in a chair, she added, "I know you enjoy coffee, I'd offer you some. But, the last time I got you coffee, it didn't work out so well for me."<br>Tony smirked, "God, Claire you're something else. I can't imagine anyone else joking about that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>One minute I adored Tony, the next I wanted him to suffer. I was right there along with Claire as far as emotional whip lash. Aleatha Romig is an actual genius when it comes to creating a character that evokes both intense passion and hatred. One minute I was soooo Team Harry (just need to mention here; how adorable is Harry?!) and then Tony would come along and I'd be pining for a Tony/Claire HEA!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's documented, when a person is forbidden something, once it's available, they tend to overindulge."<br>Tony met her gaze, his tone a sultry melody, "Before it is made available, a person may dream of it, long for it, and fantasize about it. Especially if they once had it and know how amazing it is."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Tony is such a fabulous character! He is sexy, tortured, broken, unexpectedly sensitive, protective, utterly insane at times and you learn to love every side of him, light and dark. Somehow, the fact that he started off as such a dark soul, makes his admission of love to Claire all the more heart wrenching.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I have made some bad decisions... and done some things I regret in my life... but without a doubt... what I regret the most... is divorcing you. If you tell me there is hope, that one day you'll be Mrs. Rawlings again, I will wait."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The are so many twists and turns and unexpected findings that you just can't possibly predict this book. That is one of the things that keeps you reading. What with the addition of Sophie, Derek, Harry, Phil, etc. you just have no idea what the next chapter, or page, even, is going to throw at you.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Tony lifted his glass and proposed a toast, "To you, the only person in this world, who can keep me on my toes."<br>Claire held her glass.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And the ultimate twist at the end, oh myyyyy GOD!!! I was preparing myself for the unexpected! I knew Aleatha Romig was going to try and rip the rug from under my feet and I wanted to catch her out... but I didn't! It was like a punch to the gut! Oh my God. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>No matter how much he loved her <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and her child, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> his need to fulfill his promise to Nathaniel would always prevail.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>How in the hell am I ever going to wait so long for book no. 3?!!!! I need it <i>now</i>! Like, right now!<br><br>Truth had my heart racing, breaking, melting and palpating, my mind spinning, my palms sweating and poor tired little brain working over time. It is seriously intense but so so so good. I can't recommend it enough. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Tony squeezed her hand and whispered, "It's as beautiful as I remember."<br>"Have you been here - recently?"<br>"No, I'd be lost without you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>It worries me that Consequences takes a while to get going, so people might throw the towel in too early. If that describes you, don't! I promise you with all my heart, it is worth it. It is an incredible book and will take you on such a journey! <br><br>I'm off to add Convicted to my list of 'Can't Wait Fors' of 2013 and Truth to my favourites shelf!<br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15254855106518681237" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=how-could-i-not-delve-into-this-cra">how-could-i-not-delve-into-this-cra</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer447125629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17045266743143850125"><i>
  <b>What a treat!</b>
</i><br/><br/>But before I tell you about this book, I have to tell you about the Consequences Series Support Group here on GR. They have ongoing buddy reads for these books and reading in a group makes the experience even better, imho. Here's the link: <br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/83457-the-consequences-series-group-reads-group-therapy-group-hugs'>http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/8...</a><br/><br/><b>This book is quite brilliant and I highly, highly recommend it for any reader who would normally enjoy a dark romance and doesn't require her reading material to be morally, emotionally or socially appro</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17045266743143850125" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>What a treat!</b>
</i><br /><br />But before I tell you about this book, I have to tell you about the Consequences Series Support Group here on GR. They have ongoing buddy reads for these books and reading in a group makes the experience even better, imho. Here's the link: <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/83457-the-consequences-series-group-reads-group-therapy-group-hugs">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/8...</a><br /><br /><b>This book is quite brilliant and I highly, highly recommend it for any reader who would normally enjoy a dark romance and doesn't require her reading material to be morally, emotionally or socially appropriate.</b><br /><br />I was obsessed with this book for the day and a half (and much of one sleepless night) it took me to gobble it up. For that alone, I want to give it 5 stars. However, there were flaws so I don't feel I can do that. I will probably come back and add that 5th star in a couple of days if I can't stop thinking about it. Its highly readable and gripping and shocking... just delicious. <br />ETA: Had to do it. Please refer to the fifth gleaming star at the top.<br /><br />This book is practically unreviewable for me. There is just no way to capture its story or my reading experience, but I will at least try to say something helpful.<br />Here goes: <br /><br />It might be helpful to know this is a mixed-genre novel. It has a Psychological Thriller feeling to it because it tells a story about the battle between a protagonist and antagonist which plays out like a battle of wits and is dark and disturbing. It also has a strong Romantic Suspense quality in which a sassy heroine is plunked into a dangerous situation and has to figure her way out. There's a lot of plot surprises and developments. There's help from some sexy male characters and there's definitely relationship development going on*. All this is wrapped up in the new mind-fu*kery genre (isn't that the name of this captive, non-con, not-quite-BDSM, power dynamic stuff in which the heroes are actually the "problem" but can be heroic in a pinch?). If not, that's what I'm calling it until someone gives it a proper name.<br /><br />For those who may have been a bit yuck or meh about the first book in this series, I want to encourage that you will not find any of the same writing issues in this one. Do yourself a favor- pick it up right now. Read it today. Do not pass go!<br />I consider <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12368985.Consequences__Consequences___1_" title="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Consequences</a> to be a prequel to the "big show" (which is this book right here). <br />Word.<br /><br />*I got a bit of genre definition guidance from bookcountry.com<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17045266743143850125" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText6961566320757101662" style="display:none"><blockquote>*** Spoiler free review ***</blockquote><i>

</i><br><br><blockquote>

    <b>“Move, countermove, the game continued.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381529449i/4987620.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Can you imagine, being an out of work meteorologist, working as a bartender, and falling in love with one of the countries billionaires?”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>
    <i>“What woman wouldn’t love to suddenly have Claire Rawlings life?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381692382i/5196060._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There's a menagerie of characters in this series, they all have their place and add to the development and suspense of the story..... and in my head, the question I kept asking myself was.....<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381692083i/5195468._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Truth is the second part in this intelligently written series and the tangled web created by Aleatha Romig continued to grip me and blow my mind..... It's not just simply about the relationship between Claire and Tony..... There's so much more going on, the past, the present, the thought of what will be in the future.....??? But, it's Tony and Claire that tugged at my heart and kept me on the edge of my seat for practically the entire book. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381747482i/5263910._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“No man chooses evil because it is evil; he only mistakes it for happiness, the good he seeks. – Mary Wollstonecraft.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381674020i/5175262.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The emergence of Claire’s defiance, independence and strength gave a new dimension to this story of superb substance….… Do NOT think it's a series about a week heroine because it's quite the opposite, her character never failed to disappoint me; she's a fantastic heroine caught in a web.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381529449i/4987621.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>”…charming, loving, friendly…” </i>
</b> Tony Rawlings.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The frightening domineering man was much easier to resist than the sensual, apologetic one. “</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He could be irresistible…... I certainly found him so.... ♥ I've loved him from the start of this series.... <b>“Do not disappoint me.”</b><br><i>....And I will keep the faith.... Tony..... </i><b>PLEASE don't let me down....</b><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“…..it would never be over.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Without a BR on this book I may have gone crazy!! I think Mo and I spent as much time talking about it, looking back at our highlights, and coming up with theories as we did reading. I LOVED every damn minute!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381698268i/5201291._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“All secrets are deep. All secrets become dark. That’s in the nature of secrets.” ~ Cory Doctorow</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b><i>”………I have loved you since before you knew my name.” ~ Tony</i></b><i> My heart loves him!!!</i>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>
  <b>“It wasn’t supposed to be that way.”</b>
</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>***“I think we need to proceed with caution.”***</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>BR.... thank you ladies ♥<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7481834972137230419"><b>What lies behind <i><u>Appearance</u></i> is usually another <i><u>Appearance</u></i>.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398041i/768779._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>The saga continues..........</b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Anthony Rawlings</u>
</b>: The <b>diabolical character</b> whose <i>
  <b>true</b>

  <b>consequences</b>
</i> so monstrous that it had left me <b>stunned, gaping and <i>still</i> with shock</b>......is once again not who he truly seems to be.<br/><br/>I had been <b><i>sooo</i> sure</b> that in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070018.Truth__Consequences___2_' title='Truth (Consequences, #2) by Aleatha Romig' rel='nofollow noopener'>Truth</a> he would <b>receive his comeuppance</b> and would face the consequences of <i>his actions</i> and he d</span>
  <span id="freeText7481834972137230419" style="display:none"><b>What lies behind <i><u>Appearance</u></i> is usually another <i><u>Appearance</u></i>.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398041i/768779._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The saga continues..........</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Anthony Rawlings</u>
</b>: The <b>diabolical character</b> whose <i>
  <b>true</b>
</i> face had been revealed by the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12368985.Consequences__Consequences___1_" title="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Consequences</a>.....whose <b>vendetta for vengeance</b> had led to <i>
  <b>consequences</b>
</i> so monstrous that it had left me <b>stunned, gaping and <i>still</i> with shock</b>......is once again not who he truly seems to be.<br><br>I had been <b><i>sooo</i> sure</b> that in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070018.Truth__Consequences___2_" title="Truth (Consequences, #2) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Truth</a> he would <b>receive his comeuppance</b> and would face the consequences of <i>his actions</i> and he does but just not the way I'd thought........<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Reading this book was like <b>walking in a room whose end seemed so close and yet as soon as you think you're near it, it would go farther away......</b><br><br><i><b>Things are not always what they seem</b>; the first appearance deceives many. The intelligence of a few perceives what has been <b>carefully hidden</b>.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398041ra/768781.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So true and I had forgotten that <b>the truth as it appears may not turn out to be <i>the truth</i></b>......that everything as it <b>appears may not be in reality the same</b>......that <b>the players, the chess pieces, the opponents</b>...no one was as they <b>
  <i>appeared to be</i>
</b>........<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398041i/768782.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>New players, cunning subterfuge, shocking revelations, and an unknown opponent whose moves changes the dynamics of the story and whose presence everyone is unaware of.....this story has it all.....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398041i/768783.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story begins with unforeseen circumstances leading to Claire's release and from then on, people, it's <b>a roller coaster ride in the dark.......because <i>nothing is as it seems</i>.....</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b>Claire</b>, a <i>
  <b>mighty</b>
</i> woman....who appears submissive and meek but proves that she is definitely more than that....who rises once again....just not in the way I had expected....<i>
  <b>A thing long expected takes the form of the unexpected when at last it comes.</b>
</i>.....I should have known.<br><br><i>
  <b>Change alone is eternal, perpetual, immortal.</b>
</i> And who would have thought that my <b>feelings would change <i>so drastically</i></b> regarding the man who I had considered <b>the villain, the monster of the story</b>? I definitely hadn't! <b>Call me crazy because I'm <i>in love</i>......with Anthony Rawlings!</b><br><br>This is so...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398041ra/768785.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As <b>astounding and amazing</b> it may sound, Tony had actually loved Claire.....despite his actions and the <i>resulting consequences</i>....So what led him to do the things he did?.....<b>The mystery is unraveled <i>slowly and slowly</i>....the enigma called Anthony Rawlings is revealed but that is not all.....</b> <br><br><i>Tony’s realization hit months ago when he realized it didn’t matter if she were dressed in designer gowns with perfect hair and perfect makeup or newly awake with no makeup and tussled hair. He no longer saw the difference. For a man who valued outward appearance as much as Anthony Rawlings, that insight was shocking.</i><br><br><i>....For the first time in his life he’d dared to believe in happily-ever-after.He learned at a young age it was unattainable. Therefore, he’d never even tried... until Claire.</i><br><br><i>...His words were barely audible. That was all right; they weren’t intended for anyone except the woman who wasn’t there. “I’m so sorry... for everything... why? ... why did you leave me?” As the tears coated his cheeks he told himself, <u>Anthony Rawlings doesn’t cry. He doesn’t apologize, and he doesn’t cry...</u></i><br><br>Oh God....after this <b>how can anyone resist him?</b>.....<b>Move over 50 shades...there's a new man in town...Tony (there are so many shades, facets of his personality that counting them is pretty much redundant)...</b>*sigh*....<br><br>This what my Tony looks like....<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783750i/449598._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But it's <b>not over people....the unknown is still out there and no one knows....</b><i>-There are known knowns. These are things we know that we know. There are known unknowns. That is to say, there are things that we know we don't know. But there are also unknown unknowns. There are things we don't know we don't know.</i>-.....you'll find out.<br><br>So don't miss this <b>opportunity to find out the <i>Truth</i>....fasten your seat belts and prepare yourself for the ride....venture into the dark without the flashlight(because it's not gonna help you anyway :P)....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398041i/768786.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do I need to say more?....<b>just read and find out <u><i>because all that appears in this review is not as it seems to be</i></u>....</b>. ;P</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10313470758021378280"><i>re-read April 2019</i> <br/><br/><b>5 +++++++ Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/itsallhappening_zps3b169uvb.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>The web is just getting more tangled, with every answer we get we are left with more questions. I think this is the book that made me fall for Tony hard, as we are shown bits of who he truly is and why he did some of the horrific things he had done in book 1. Again there is just to much going on in these books to even try and explain it and this book is even more intense and full on than book 1.<br/><br/>I still feel the same for this book as I did in 2015, I think I </span>
  <span id="freeText10313470758021378280" style="display:none"><i>re-read April 2019</i> <br><br><b>5 +++++++ Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/itsallhappening_zps3b169uvb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>The web is just getting more tangled, with every answer we get we are left with more questions. I think this is the book that made me fall for Tony hard, as we are shown bits of who he truly is and why he did some of the horrific things he had done in book 1. Again there is just to much going on in these books to even try and explain it and this book is even more intense and full on than book 1.<br><br>I still feel the same for this book as I did in 2015, I think I love it even more now. I have read so many books and series since I first read this and I can say with all honesty that this is still in my top 10 series ever read!!<br><br>I have to say how amazingly written this series is. Filled with angst, intrigue, suspense and drama it is why I will always 1-click any dark book Aleatha publishes, she is the queen of the dark twisted alphas. I also want to give props to the narrator, at first I was bummed that it was just a lady narrator reading all the characters but after a while it didn't bother me. She needs recognition as these books have so many characters and she plays them all well.<br><br><a href="https://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/brilliant_zpsfvacnai6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1554977356ra/27346895.gif" alt=" photo brilliant_zpsfvacnai6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>2015 review</i><br><br><b>5 MIGHTY STARS</b><br><br>I LOVE this series it is in my top 10!!!! The books are long but because they are written so well and there is so much going on the pages turn easily. I am skipping the companion books because I just need to know what happens :-).<br><br>Anton/Anthony Rowls/Rowlings makes you hate, love, fear and lust all in one page. I like books that contain hot and steamy bedroom scenes so it surprises me that I love this book and it doesn't have the explicit scenes in which an erotic reader is accustomed but seriously who cares when the writing and story is so FANTASTIC.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7522167166989253343"><b>WTH!!! WOW!!!! She finally grew some lady balls and stood up for herself. She came to her senses and wanted to get revenge against Anthony for all the horrible things he did her. She even develo</span>
  <span id="freeText7522167166989253343" style="display:none"><b>WTH!!! WOW!!!! ONCE AGAIN I'M SPEECHLESS!!!!</b> <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400976ra/777555.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I feel so emotional drained with this book. Once again the ending was so jaw dropping. When I thought I had this book figured out something totally different happens again. I'm left feeling like....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400976ra/777556.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Another MindFuck Ending</b><br><br>In the beginning of this book, I loved the new Claire. She finally grew some lady balls and stood up for herself. She came to her senses and wanted to get revenge against Anthony for all the horrible things he did her. I wanted Claire to keep fighting back and make Anthony beg for forgiveness, but that didn't happen. She became weak and helpless Claire all over again and now I just think she is so stupid. I seriously don't feel sorry for her anymore.<br><br>A big round of applause goes to Aleatha Romig...<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400976ra/777557.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Mrs. Romig did the impossible. I still don't like him, but I don't hate him anymore if that makes any sense. Don’t get it twisted!! He is still a psychopath though, but with a sweet side lol<br><br>This book was amazing!!! My hat goes off to you Mrs. Romig. Because the second time you make it, it is not a mistake, it is a choice."<br><br>"Your memory is a monster; you forget- it doesn't. It simply files things away. It keeps things for you, or hides things from you- and summons them to your recall with a will of its own. You think you have a memory; it has you!"<br><br>"We gain strength, and courage, and confidence by each experience in which we really stop to look fear in the face....we must do that which we think we cannot."</span>

<div id="review_435557179" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/435557179" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/435557179?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=thriller-suspense">thriller-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer435557179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2164257027791247800"><br/><i>The truth is rarely pure and never simple.</i> -- Oscar Wilde<br/><br/>TRUTH is an intricately woven plot that begins with Consequences. It would be difficult for a new reader to understand the story without reading the first book. Therefore, before reading Truth, I highly recommend reading Consequences first. You do not want to miss out on a huge chunk of the plot and prior events that happen in Consequences! <br/><br/>Anthony and Claire have a complex relationship - which is a HUGE understatement. There is absolutely</span>
  <span id="freeText2164257027791247800" style="display:none"><br /><i>The truth is rarely pure and never simple.</i> -- Oscar Wilde<br /><br />TRUTH is an intricately woven plot that begins with Consequences. It would be difficult for a new reader to understand the story without reading the first book. Therefore, before reading Truth, I highly recommend reading Consequences first. You do not want to miss out on a huge chunk of the plot and prior events that happen in Consequences! <br /><br />Anthony and Claire have a complex relationship - which is a HUGE understatement. There is absolutely nothing normal with the way they met or the way their relationship formed. In Consequences, Anthony kidnapped, violated, isolated, and controlled Claire. What started out as a strategic plan of revenge, turned into a very untraditional romance that not only ripped out my heart out but shredded it as well. I was frustrated, angry, and seeing RED by the end of Consequences. There was only one thing on my mind when I began reading Truth: I wanted justice. No, scratch that, I wanted REVENGE. I wanted Claire to get her life back and get her due repentance for what Anthony did to her. <br /><br />Truth opens up with Claire being pardoned from prison after spending 14 months in jail for the attempted murder of her husband. A crime she didn't commit. With her newfound freedom, she begins to build her life again. This time, she has an agenda. She wants vengeance against the man who ruined her life. She has questions and she wants answers. <br /><br />As the story progresses, Claire begins to realize that the truth is even more complicated than she ever imagined. And as she begins to investigate and unravel part of the truth, she realizes appearances aren't always what they seem. She should know—she played the game for over two years with Anthony when she was in his possession. <br /><br />Claire's strength and determination is admirable. She's determined to reveal the mystery that makes up Anthony Rawlings. When he does come into the picture, she finds it difficult to trust herself around him. She vacillates between feelings of love and hate. And, as we all know from reading Consequences, Anthony is easy to love and definitely easy to hate. However, she cannot forget what has been done to her. And Anthony, the conniving, controlling, manipulator he is, is determined to make her his again. <br /><br /><i>None of this made sense. Claire wanted Tony to pay for his sins. She wanted to bring him down. And, and...and she wanted what they had, but more...better.</i><br /><br />For the first 70% of the book, I fought this story. I wanted something completely different. I was unsure where the story was taking me and I felt helpless reading it as it unfolded. It made no sense as to why Miz Romig was leading me down a road I didn't want to go. And then, somewhere along the way, she turned the tables. She made me realize WHY I shouldn't have fought against the story. So at that point, I put my seat belt on and held on tight as I rode this wild and emotional ride. <br /><br />The questions that are probably on everyone's mind: Is Anthony guilty of his crimes? Is Anthony redeemable? Is there a future for Claire and Anthony? Does Claire get her revenge? I'm sure there are even more questions the readers want to know. Truth does not leave you hanging. Answers will be given. And, oh, what a huge web of truth and lies have been woven. <br /><br /><i>Things are not always what they seem; the first appearance deceives many. The intelligence of a few, perceives what has been carefully hidden.</i> -- Roman poet Phaedrus<br /><br />The unpredictable ending once again left me stunned. Everything that is revealed up until that point began to sink in and I put two and two together. I can only imagine the conflicted feelings for those who love Tony and those who hate Tony. Truth will infuriate you, push your boundaries, and leave you begging for Convicted. And if you think you know the truth, I guarantee, you are probably wrong. I know I was. This boundary pushing psychological thriller will keep you on the edge of your seat the whole time. You DO NOT want to miss reading Truth.<br /><br /><br /><i>Arc was kindly provided by Aleatha Romig</i><br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2164257027791247800" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer437611795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15043626260852176178"><a href='http://photobucket.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799298i/652617._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo Truthbanner_zps0c72e21d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://bookienookiereviews.blogspot.com/2013/08/blog-tour-review-giveaway-truth-by.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>View Updated Review & Enter to Win!</a><br/><br/><br/>How EXACTLY does one go about writing a review about such a mysterious and complicated story line without giving anything away? I’m not sure, because I am still trying to figure that out…<br/><br/>After pondering TRUTH and everything that has transpired in the Rawlings’ world, I’m not certain I am in any better frame of mind to review this book any more than I was a few days ago, but I am going to try. I do think it is important to note to the readers that this is a </span>
  <span id="freeText15043626260852176178" style="display:none"><a href="http://photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799298i/652617._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Truthbanner_zps0c72e21d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://bookienookiereviews.blogspot.com/2013/08/blog-tour-review-giveaway-truth-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">View Updated Review &amp; Enter to Win!</a><br><br><br>How EXACTLY does one go about writing a review about such a mysterious and complicated story line without giving anything away? I’m not sure, because I am still trying to figure that out…<br><br>After pondering TRUTH and everything that has transpired in the Rawlings’ world, I’m not certain I am in any better frame of mind to review this book any more than I was a few days ago, but I am going to try. I do think it is important to note to the readers that this is a trilogy that you have to read in order, so if you are thinking about picking this book up, make sure you have read CONSEQUENCES first!<br><br>To say that Claire and Tony have a complicated relationship is quite possibly the understatement of the century. Since, by now, you all have read the first book in the trilogy, CONSEQUENCES, you are aware that Claire and Tony’s relationship did not begin as most “normal” love affairs do. In an effort to right the wrongs of the past by exacting revenge on those near and dear to the offenders, Tony kidnaps and brutalizes Claire for a period of 2 years. To the general public, Claire appears to have it all as Tony’s wife. After all, Tony is a debonair businessman any woman would be lucky to have as a companion and most certainly a prime catch as a husband, but we all know that looks can be very deceiving. <br><br>In TRUTH, author, Aleatha Romig continues to torment readers with the sweet torture of Claire and Tony’s story, a story that is so intricately woven you can scarcely blink an eye or you might miss something crucial. <br><br>Following Claire’s incarceration for the attempted murder of her husband, an angel bestows a great gift upon her in the form of a pardon. After serving 14 months in prison for a crime she probably did not commit, she is released from prison and granted a pardon from her crime, meaning that she is forgiven and in the eyes of the law, it never occurred – it is expunged from her record. I am saying she “probably did not commit this crime” because you never know what kind of monkey wrench Romig, is planning to throw into the final book, CONVICTED, being the wicked tale-teller she is, I cannot begin to fathom what she has up her sleeve…anyhoo, I digress… <br><br>Embracing her newfound gift of freedom, Claire endeavors to rebuild her life and uncover answers to the questions that have been weighing on the minds of all the players in this very risky game of life and revenge. Is the truth worth risking her life? CONSEQUENCES demonstrated that not all is not as it seems in the world surrounding Anthony Rawlings. TRUTH further solidifies that perception is not always reality. Can Claire distinguish friend from foe in time to save herself and the ones she loves? Only time will tell. <br><br>What an exhilarating ride! The players in this game of TRUTH were intense and charismatic, although new people were introduced, our old favorites we love to hate got plenty of face-time, namely Tony. If you like a twisty plot with loads of mysteries around every corner, then TRUTH is a must-read! It’s a thrilling and thought-provoking psychological thriller at it’s best! The wait for the final installment is going to be agonizing…2014 cannot come soon enough… <br><br>✳✳ <i>Copy provided by the author/publisher for an honest review.</i><br>✳✳ Reviewed on <a href="http://bookienookiereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">I ♥ Bookie Nookie Reviews</a><br><br>___________________________________________________<br>If you like this type of book, you might enjoy one of these groups. Check us out!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/42800" rel="nofollow noopener">Menage Readers</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/2344" rel="nofollow noopener">Erotic Enchants</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/49647.Bookie_Nookie_s_Erotic_eBook_Exchange" rel="nofollow noopener">Bookie Nookie's Erotic Lending Group</a><br></span>
