        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591134971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9096580861222591533"><b> 6 MIND BLOWING STARS!</b> <br/><blockquote>
  <i>Could it be possible to hate and love someone too?</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381355123i/4754943.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><blockquote>
  <i>You cannot make the same mistake twice. Because the second time you make it, it is a choice.</i>
</blockquote><br/>Claire and Tony's mind blowing story drove me to the brink of insanity. So many <i>TRUTHS</i> were revealed in this book. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12368985.Consequences__Consequences___1_' title='Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig' rel='nofollow noopener'>Consequences</a> left me bored until the last 11% where the story took a major twist. <u>Truth</u> gripped me right from the start and became unputdownable. <br/><br/>Ms. Romig did an excellent job creating a story full of mystery a</span>
  <span id="freeText9096580861222591533" style="display:none"><b> 6 MIND BLOWING STARS!</b> <br><blockquote>
  <i>Could it be possible to hate and love someone too?</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381355123i/4754943.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><blockquote>
  <i>You cannot make the same mistake twice. Because the second time you make it, it is a choice.</i>
</blockquote><br>Claire and Tony's mind blowing story drove me to the brink of insanity. So many <i>TRUTHS</i> were revealed in this book. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12368985.Consequences__Consequences___1_" title="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Consequences</a> left me bored until the last 11% where the story took a major twist. <u>Truth</u> gripped me right from the start and became unputdownable. <br><br>Ms. Romig did an excellent job creating a story full of mystery and suspense. Only two other series I have read have been able to create a <b>master puzzle </b>that keeps your attention and has you on the edge of your seat: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/79635-the-original-sinners" rel="nofollow noopener">The Original Sinners</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/85015-love-me-with-lies" rel="nofollow noopener">Love Me With Lies.</a><br><br>For all those who I told that they were crazy for being Team Tony...I'm officially apologizing!<b> I was wrong. Please forgive me;</b><i> Kara, Renee, Christy, Monika, Jaqueline (and anyone else I missed).</i> Friends still?<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16100228.Consequences__Consequences___1_" title="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1350858737s/16100228.jpg" alt="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070018.Truth__Consequences___2_" title="Truth (Consequences, #2) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1358340650s/16070018.jpg" alt="Truth (Consequences, #2) by Aleatha Romig" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150996.Convicted__Consequences___3_" title="Convicted (Consequences, #3) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1378036825s/16150996.jpg" alt="Convicted (Consequences, #3) by Aleatha Romig" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Cliffhangers. Continuing story. <br><br><i>Novellas:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18660518.Behind_His_Eyes___Consequences__Consequences___4_" title="Behind His Eyes - Consequences (Consequences, #4) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png" alt="Behind His Eyes - Consequences (Consequences, #4) by Aleatha Romig" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18660519.Behind_His_Eyes___Truth__Consequences___5_" title="Behind His Eyes - Truth (Consequences, #5) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png" alt="Behind His Eyes - Truth (Consequences, #5) by Aleatha Romig" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png" alt="Behind His Eyes - Convicted (Consequences, #6) by Aleatha Romig" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(#4) (#5) (#6)<br>Retelling of significant scenes from Tony's POV.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/446803454?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=mind-fuckery">mind-fuckery</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer446803454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8715096159691738530">Re-read 10-10-13 in prep for Convicted. 4.5 "crazy ride" stars!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=e2ef69b3c977649e1ee85bfb2527ced0_zps5a8c8a00.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381455422i/4890133._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I re-read this book in prep for Convicted. I remembered it had lots of characters and a rather complicated plot, so I decided a refresher was prudent. I'm happy I did too. Not a whole lot of my opinion has changed since the first read... It's still very mysterious, captivating, shocking at times. Towards the end, we start to get some answers to all the secrets hidden behind Tony and each character's involvement in his plan. A lot</span>
  <span id="freeText8715096159691738530" style="display:none">Re-read 10-10-13 in prep for Convicted. 4.5 "crazy ride" stars!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=e2ef69b3c977649e1ee85bfb2527ced0_zps5a8c8a00.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381455422i/4890133._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I re-read this book in prep for Convicted. I remembered it had lots of characters and a rather complicated plot, so I decided a refresher was prudent. I'm happy I did too. Not a whole lot of my opinion has changed since the first read... It's still very mysterious, captivating, shocking at times. Towards the end, we start to get some answers to all the secrets hidden behind Tony and each character's involvement in his plan. A lot of shockers are thrown in also. Moving on....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=4167ffd67b638ddb8918b46166e9fb14_zps48efbb06.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381455422i/4890134._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Previous review.....<br>I didn't think Ms Romig could do it but she surely did! Holy Moses! I did not see that coming! Loved loved loved this . It's on my favorites shelf for sure. I had no clue. So many twists to the story. This needs to be made into a movie! She kept me captivated, at the edge of my seat. My hands are trembling just typing this. It is impossible to review this book thoroughly without giving away parts of the plot and answers that lie in the end so I'll be vague. New people come into play with this book and all tie together in the end. There's still a "what's going to happen next" component but I'm happy with the end as it stands. I can't wait until Convicted is out. Write fast Ms Romig. You have a gift! I never thought my hatred of Tony could lesson.....but it did. BRAVO!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer455871669" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13283111365474640151"><b>WHAT THE HELL JUST HAPPENED?</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397633ra/767463.gif' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, well, well this sequel DOES NOT disappoint! Truth was a fast paced heart pounding read. My opinions of old characters especially Antony Rawlings have changed…maybe I even like him. Yep, I know crazy but true. <br/><br/>Claire Nichols seeks revenge and the truth this time around. She has put on her detective hat and made some new friends. She has decided to figuratively play game of chess with Tony. This game between Claire and Tony gets pretty intense and definitely excit</span>
  <span id="freeText13283111365474640151" style="display:none"><b>WHAT THE HELL JUST HAPPENED?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397633ra/767463.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, well, well this sequel DOES NOT disappoint! Truth was a fast paced heart pounding read. My opinions of old characters especially Antony Rawlings have changed…maybe I even like him. Yep, I know crazy but true. <br><br>Claire Nichols seeks revenge and the truth this time around. She has put on her detective hat and made some new friends. She has decided to figuratively play game of chess with Tony. This game between Claire and Tony gets pretty intense and definitely exciting. Both characters try to win but their “mighty” connection gets in the way. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes I think I'm an opponent. Other times I think he believes I'm the prize."</i>
</b><br><br>By the end of Truth, you will have most of the answers you were seeking in Consequences. Please be prepared to <b>scream and shout</b> at some of Claire’s decisions. All comes together in the end in a brilliant crazy way!<br><br><b>
  <i>”God she hated him, and not!”</i>
</b><i></i> <br><br>I want to give a shout out to my favorite character of the two books…<b>John Vanderol</b> Love You!! <br><br>I’m anxiously awaiting the third book of this series to see what awaits this couple.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('uvzkwOmN0pXUaUcBOutlxLVJx8XZbCManpP2+SLKOTGc1PVBn5Mp1+0r9DLHfG6Ta5GiQlw4crn5uj7ZpPJjbQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('72EjWBAEj6r8q3WdyaMVxcjw9yxj8Q/mE8rPRf7EY7/JSTLZZhp06MXpxq40NB6SFiiSq+alXkV04wdlePw54w==')})
  }
//]]>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/5131072.Aleatha_Romig">About Aleatha Romig</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/5131072.Aleatha_Romig"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1445297443p3/5131072.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2947840210206324064">Aleatha Romig is a New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today bestselling author who lives in Indiana, USA. She grew up in Mishawaka, graduated from Indiana University, and is currently living south of Indianapolis. Aleatha has raised three children with her high school sweetheart and husband of over thirty years. Before she became a full-time author, she worked days as a dental hygienist </span>
  <span id="freeText2947840210206324064" style="display:none">Aleatha Romig is a New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today bestselling author who lives in Indiana, USA. She grew up in Mishawaka, graduated from Indiana University, and is currently living south of Indianapolis. Aleatha has raised three children with her high school sweetheart and husband of over thirty years. Before she became a full-time author, she worked days as a dental hygienist and spent her nights writing. Now, when she's not imagining mind-blowing twists and turns, she likes to spend her time with her family and friends. Her other pastimes include reading and creating heroes/anti-heroes who haunt your dreams!<br /><br />Aleatha released her first novel, CONSEQUENCES, in August of 2011. CONSEQUENCES became a bestselling series with five novels and two companions released from 2011 through 2015. The compelling and epic story of Anthony and Claire Rawlings has graced more than half a million e-readers. Aleatha released the first of her series TALES FROM THE DARK SIDE, INSIDIOUS, in the fall of 2014. These stand-alone thrillers continue Aleatha's twisted style with an increase in heat. <br /><br />In the fall of 2015, Aleatha moved headfirst into the world of dark romantic suspense saga with the release of BETRAYAL, the first of her five-novel INFIDELITY series that has taken the reading world by storm. She also began her traditional publishing career with Thomas and Mercer. Her books INTO THE LIGHT and AWAY FROM THE DARK were published through this mystery/thriller publisher in 2016.<br /><br />In the spring of 2017, Aleatha released her first stand-alone, fun, and sexy romantic comedy PLUS ONE, followed by ONE NIGHT, and ANOTHER ONE. Her range of genres includes erotic romance novellas in her INDULGENCE series.<br /><br />Aleatha returned to her dark roots in 2018 with WEB OF SIN, a dark romantic trilogy with an all new anti-hero. The Sparrow Webs continued with TANGLED WEB, WEB OF DESIRE, and soon DANGEROUS WEB. <br /><br />Aleatha is a "Published Author's Network" member of the Romance Writers of America, NINC, and PEN America. She is represented by Kevan Lyon of Marsal Lyon Literary Agency. Her marketing is represented by Wildfire Marketing.<br /></span>

Claire has no understanding of why she\'s there, but it\'s been made abundantly clear--she is now his acquisition and every action has consequences.\n\nLearn the rules to survive.\n\nFacing incomprehensible circumstances, Claire must learn to survive her new reality--every aspect of her livelihood depends upon the tall, dark-eyed tycoon who is a true master of deception. Driven by unknown demons, he has no tolerance for imperfection, in any aspect of his life, including his recent acquisition. Anthony may appear to the world as a handsome, benevolent businessman, but in reality Claire knows firsthand that he\'s a menacing, controlling captor with very strict rules: do as you\'re told, public failure is not an option, and appearances are of the utmost importance.\n\nCaptivate the captor.\n\nTo fit together the pieces of the puzzle, Claire must follow his rules. Will her plan work, or will Anthony become enthralled by Claire\'s beauty, resilience, and determination, changing the game forever? If that happens, will either of them survive the consequences?\n\nNobody ever did or ever will escape the consequences of his choices.--Alfred A.
